## üìù VISI MISI

### Visi ‚úÖ
Menjadi digital agency terdepan di Indonesia yang memberdayakan UMKM dan brand lokal untuk bersaing secara global melalui solusi digital inovatif dan teknologi terkini.

### Misi (5 Poin) ‚úÖ
1. Menyediakan solusi digital berkualitas tinggi dengan harga terjangkau untuk UMKM Indonesia
2. Membantu bisnis lokal go digital dengan strategi dan teknologi yang tepat
3. Memberikan training dan edukasi digital untuk meningkatkan kapabilitas tim client
4. Membangun ekosistem kerja sama dengan freelancer berbakat melalui sistem komisi yang adil
5. Menjaga kepuasan client melalui support 24/7 dan garansi kepuasan 100%

## ‚ùì FAQ (7 Pertanyaan) ‚úÖ

**Q1: Berapa lama proses pembuatan website?**  
A: Website standar 5-8 halaman kami kerjakan dalam 7-14 hari kerja. E-commerce: 14-21 hari. Custom system: 30-45 hari. Tergantung kompleksitas dan responsifnya klien memberikan feedback.

**Q2: Apakah ada jaminan website akan ranking di Google?**  
A: Kami tidak bisa menjamin ranking karena itu tergantung algoritma Google. Tapi kami pastikan website Anda SEO-friendly dengan on-page optimization, technical SEO, dan strategy konten yang tepat.

**Q3: Apa yang termasuk dalam paket website?**  
A: Paket sudah include domain, hosting, SSL, design responsive, basic SEO, contact form, dan maintenance selama periode kontrak. Lihat detail paket di halaman pricing.

**Q4: Berapa biaya jika ingin custom features?**  
A: Tergantung kompleksitas fitur. Bisa mulai dari 500rb untuk integrasi sederhana hingga jutaan untuk custom development. Chat kami untuk konsultasi gratis.

**Q5: Apakah saya bisa update website sendiri?**  
A: Ya! Semua website kami dilengkapi admin panel yang mudah digunakan. Kami juga sediakan training gratis 2 jam untuk menggunakan CMS.

**Q6: Apa itu free demo 24 jam?**  
A: Kami akan membuat preview website Anda dalam 24 jam tanpa charge. Jika Anda suka, lanjut ke proses development. Jika tidak, tidak ada biaya sama sekali.

**Q7: Bagaimana support setelah website launch?**  
A: Support 24/7 via WhatsApp. Semua paket sudah include maintenance selama periode kontrak. Setelah itu, bisa extend maintenance bulanan dengan harga terjangkau.

## üîê BUSINESS MODEL - 3 ROLE SYSTEM

### 1Ô∏è‚É£ ADMIN (Devin Prasetyo Hermawan)
**Full Control Access:**
- Dashboard analytics (revenue, orders, traffic)
- Manage users (client, freelancer) - CRUD, suspend, bulk actions
- Manage orders - assign freelancer, update status, upload files
- Payment verification - approve/reject payment proof
- Manage services & packages - pricing, features, visibility
- Manage portfolio - 50 demo showcase
- Review moderation - approve/reject reviews
- **Withdrawal management** - approve freelancer withdrawal (min 50K)
- Settings - company info, email templates, backup
- Reports - revenue, popular services, conversion rate
- **Demo Request Management** - dengan "Copy for AI" feature

### 2Ô∏è‚É£ CLIENT (Pembeli)
**Limited Access:**
- Dashboard overview - orders, invoices, payments
- **Request demo gratis** - form 26 fields super lengkap
- Order layanan - pilih service/package, checkout
- Upload payment proof - bank transfer, QRIS
- Track order progress - Pending ‚Üí In Development ‚Üí Testing ‚Üí Completed
- View invoices - download PDF, print
- Payment history - filter by date, export
- Profile management - edit info, change password
- Notifications - order updates, payment status, promo
- Support tickets - create ticket, chat with admin
- **Review & rating** - after project completed

### 3Ô∏è‚É£ FREELANCER (Mitra/Reseller)
**Mitra Access:**
- Dashboard earnings - total komisi, pending, available
- **Jual produk SITUNEO** - dapat link referral unik
- Commission tracking - **30% dari setiap project**
- **Withdrawal request** - minimal 50K, transfer ke bank
- Referral link generator - untuk share ke client
- Client list - siapa yang order dari referral
- Transaction history - detail komisi per order
- Profile management - bank info, KTP, social media
- Performance stats - total sales, conversion rate
- Notifications - ada order baru dari referral, komisi masuk

## üí∞ COMMISSION FLOW (FREELANCER)

```
1. Freelancer share link referral: 
   https://situneo.my.id?ref=FREELANCER_CODE

2. Client order via link tersebut:
   Order: Website Toko Online (Rp 2,5 juta)

3. Client bayar LUNAS:
   Status order: "Completed & Paid"

4. Komisi 30% otomatis masuk ke balance:
   Komisi: Rp 750,000 (30% dari 2,5 juta)

5. Freelancer request withdrawal (min 50K):
   Status: "Pending Approval"

6. Admin approve:
   Status: "Approved - Transfer dalam 1x24 jam"

7. Freelancer terima transfer ke bank:
   Komisi masuk rekening ‚úÖ
```

Saya telah menganalisis rekap lengkap project Situneo Digital. Berikut adalah analisis mendalam dan rekomendasi saya:

## üéØ STATUS PROJECT SAAT INI

Project Situneo Digital berada dalam tahap **"Siap Development"** dengan data perusahaan yang lengkap dan siap produksi. Beberapa halaman publik telah dibuat namun masih ada beberapa masalah yang perlu diperbaiki.

## üîç ANALISIS STRUKTUR BISNIS

### Model Bisnis 3 Peran
Sistem yang dirancang sangat komprehensif dengan 3 peran utama:
1. **Admin** - Kontrol penuh atas sistem
2. **Client** - Pembeli layanan
3. **Freelancer** - Mitra/reseller dengan komisi 30%

### Alur Komisi Freelancer
Model komisi yang dirancang sangat menarik dengan:
- Komisi 30% dari setiap project
- Minimal penarikan Rp 50.000
- Sistem referral yang terintegrasi
- Tracking komisi yang transparan

## ‚ö†Ô∏è ISU KRITIS YANG PERLU DIPERBAIKI

### 1. about.php - Variable $team Tidak Didefinisikan
Ini adalah masalah paling kritis yang akan menyebabkan error fatal pada halaman about.

### 2. Ketidakkonsistenan Nomor WhatsApp
Beberapa file masih menggunakan nomor lama `628170404594` yang harus diganti ke `6283173868915`.

### 3. Ketidakkonsistenan Email
Beberapa file masih menggunakan `info@situneo.my.id` yang harus diganti ke `vins@situneo.my.id` (utama) dan `support@situneo.my.id` (support).

## üõ†Ô∏è REKOMENDASI PERBAIKAN

### Prioritas 1: Fix Critical Issues

### Prioritas 2: Standardisasi Kontak
Buat file konfigurasi terpusat untuk semua informasi kontak:

```php
// includes/contact-config.php
define('WHATSAPP_NUMBER', '6283173868915');
define('EMAIL_UTAMA', 'vins@situneo.my.id');
define('EMAIL_SUPPORT', 'support@situneo.my.id');
define('TELEPON', '021-8880-7229');
```

## üìä ANALISIS FITUR UNGGULAN

### 1. Request Demo 24 Jam
Fitur ini sangat powerful dengan 26 field yang komprehensif dan tombol "Copy for AI" yang inovatif.

### 2. Sistem Komisi Freelancer
Model bisnis yang sangat scalable dengan komisi 30% dan sistem withdrawal yang jelas.

### 3. Pricing Calculator
Sistem kalkulasi otomatis dengan diskon untuk pembelian multiple layanan.

## üöÄ REKOMENDASI DEVELOPMENT

### Tahap 1: Fix Critical Issues (1-2 hari)
- Perbaiki variable $team di about.php
- Standardisasi nomor WhatsApp di semua file
- Standardisasi email di semua file

### Tahap 2: Complete Public Pages (3-5 hari)
- Review dan finalisasi portfolio.php
- Review dan finalisasi pricing.php
- Review dan finalisasi services.php

### Tahap 3: Authentication System (5-7 hari)
- Implementasi login/register
- Password reset functionality
- Email verification

### Tahap 4: Dashboard Development (10-14 hari)
- Client Dashboard (8 files)
- Admin Panel (17 files)
- Freelancer Dashboard (5 files)

## üí° REKOMENDASI STRATEGIS

### 1. Implementasi Progressive Web App (PWA)
Pertimbangkan untuk mengubah website menjadi PWA untuk meningkatkan user experience dan engagement.

### 2. Integrasi WhatsApp API
Implementasi WhatsApp API untuk notifikasi otomatis dan customer service yang lebih baik.

### 3. Sistem Review dan Rating
Implementasi sistem review dan rating yang lebih robust untuk meningkatkan trust factor.

### 4. Analytics Dashboard
Tambahkan analytics dashboard yang lebih komprehensif untuk tracking performance bisnis.

## üéØ KESIMPULAN

Project Situneo Digital memiliki potensi yang sangat besar dengan:
- Model bisnis yang scalable
- Fitur-fitur inovatif
- Data perusahaan yang lengkap dan profesional
- Tim yang solid

Dengan perbaikan masalah kritis dan pengembangan sesuai roadmap, project ini siap untuk go-live dalam waktu 3-4 minggu.

**Next Steps:**
1. Fix critical issues immediately
2. Complete public pages review
3. Implement authentication system
4. Develop dashboard systems
5. Integrate payment gateway
6. Go-live preparation

    <!-- Custom Scripts -->
    <script>
        // Initialize AOS
        AOS.init({
            duration: 800,
            once: true,
            offset: 100
        });
        
        // Navbar scroll effect
        window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
            const navbar = document.querySelector('.navbar');
            if (window.scrollY > 50) {
                navbar.classList.add('scrolled');
            } else {
                navbar.classList.remove('scrolled');
            }
        });
        
        // Counter animation for stats
        function animateCounter(element, target, duration = 2000) {
            const suffix = element.dataset.suffix || '';
            let current = 0;
            const isPercentage = suffix === '%';
            const numericTarget = parseInt(target.replace(/[^0-9]/g, ''));
            
            if (isNaN(numericTarget)) {
                element.textContent = target;
                return;
            }
            
            const increment = numericTarget / (duration / 16);
            const timer = setInterval(() => {
                current += increment;
                if (current >= numericTarget) {
                    element.textContent = target;
                    clearInterval(timer);
                } else {
                    element.textContent = Math.floor(current) + (suffix || '+');
                }
            }, 16);
        }
        
        // Trigger counter animation when stats section is visible
        const statsSection = document.querySelector('.stats-section');
        if (statsSection) {
            const statsObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
                entries.forEach(entry => {
                    if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                        const numbers = entry.target.querySelectorAll('.stat-number');
                        numbers.forEach(number => {
                            const target = number.textContent;
                            number.dataset.suffix = target.includes('%') ? '%' : '+';
                            animateCounter(number, target);
                        });
                        statsObserver.unobserve(entry.target);
                    }
                });
            }, { threshold: 0.5 });
            
            statsObserver.observe(statsSection);
        }
        
        // Smooth scroll for anchor links
        document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
            anchor.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                const target = document.querySelector(this.getAttribute('href'));
                if (target) {
                    const offsetTop = target.offsetTop - 80;
                    window.scrollTo({
                        top: offsetTop,
                        behavior: 'smooth'
                    });
                }
            });
        });
        
        // Parallax effect for hero section
        window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
            const hero = document.querySelector('.hero-section');
            if (hero) {
                const scrolled = window.pageYOffset;
                hero.style.transform = 'translateY(' + (scrolled * 0.5) + 'px)';
            }
        });
        
        // Log page view
        console.log('About page loaded successfully');
        console.log('Team members: <?= count($team) ?>');
        console.log('Timeline items: <?= count($timeline) ?>');
    </script>
</body>
</html>

### ASSISTANT
# üìã ANALISIS & PERBAIKAN FILE about.php

Saya telah menganalisis file about.php yang Anda kirimkan. Berikut adalah analisis lengkap dan perbaikan yang diperlukan:

## üîç ANALISIS FILE

### Status Umum
- File sudah memiliki struktur yang baik dengan desain modern
- Sudah mendukung multi-bahasa (ID/EN)
- Menggunakan AOS animation untuk efek scroll
- Sudah responsive untuk mobile

### ‚ùå MASALAH KRITIS YANG DITEMUKAN

1. **Variable $team tidak didefinisikan** (Line 282)
   - Ini akan menyebabkan error fatal saat halaman dimuat
   - Diperlukan definisi data team sebelum loop

2. **Nomor WhatsApp tidak konsisten**
   - File ini menggunakan `628170404594`
   - Seharusnya `6283173868915` sesuai data perusahaan

3. **Email tidak konsisten**
   - Footer menggunakan `info@situneo.my.id`
   - Seharusnya `vins@situneo.my.id` (utama) dan `support@situneo.my.id` (support)

## üõ†Ô∏è PERBAIKAN YANG DIPERLUKAN

    <!-- Bootstrap JS -->
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
    
    <!-- AOS Animation -->
    <script src="https://unpkg.com/aos@2.3.1/dist/aos.js"></script>
    
    <!-- Custom Scripts -->
    <script>
        // Initialize AOS
        AOS.init({
            duration: 800,
            once: true,
            offset: 100
        });
        
        // Navbar scroll effect
        window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
            const navbar = document.querySelector('.navbar');
            if (window.scrollY > 50) {
                navbar.classList.add('scrolled');
            } else {
                navbar.classList.remove('scrolled');
            }
        });
        
        // Services data
        const servicesData = <?= json_encode($services) ?>;
        
        // Cart data
        let cart = [];
        
        // Category filter
        document.querySelectorAll('.category-btn').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                // Remove active from all
                document.querySelectorAll('.category-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
                // Add active to clicked
                this.classList.add('active');
                
                const category = this.getAttribute('data-category');
                filterServices(category);
            });
        });
        
        function filterServices(category) {
            const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.service-card');
            cards.forEach(card => {
                if (category === 'all' || card.getAttribute('data-category') === category) {
                    card.style.display = 'block';
                } else {
                    card.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        }
        
        // Add to cart
        function addToCart(serviceId) {
            const service = servicesData.find(s => s.id === serviceId);
            const existingItem = cart.find(item => item.id === serviceId);
            
            if (existingItem) {
                existingItem.qty++;
            } else {
                cart.push({
                    id: service.id,
                    name: service.name,
                    price: service.price,
                    unit: service.unit,
                    qty: 1
                });
            }
            
            updateCart();
            
            // Visual feedback
            const card = document.querySelector(`.service-card[data-id="${serviceId}"]`);
            card.classList.add('added');
            setTimeout(() => card.classList.remove('added'), 300);
        }
        
        // Remove from cart
        function removeFromCart(serviceId) {
            cart = cart.filter(item => item.id !== serviceId);
            updateCart();
        }
        
        // Update quantity
        function updateQty(serviceId, qty) {
            const item = cart.find(item => item.id === serviceId);
            if (item) {
                item.qty = Math.max(1, parseInt(qty));
                updateCart();
            }
        }
        
        // Clear cart
        function clearCart() {
            if (confirm('Hapus semua item dari keranjang?')) {
                cart = [];
                updateCart();
            }
        }
        
        // Update cart display
        function updateCart() {
            const cartItems = document.getElementById('cartItems');
            const summary = document.getElementById('summary');
            const comparison = document.getElementById('packageComparison');
            
            if (cart.length === 0) {
                cartItems.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="empty-state">
                        <i class="bi bi-cart-x empty-icon"></i>
                        <div class="empty-text">
                            <strong><?= $t['empty_cart'] ?></strong><br>
                            <small><?= $t['empty_cart_desc'] ?></small>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `;
                summary.style.display = 'none';
                comparison.style.display = 'none';
                return;
            }
            
            // Show cart items
            cartItems.innerHTML = cart.map(item => `
                <div class="cart-item">
                    <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-start mb-2">
                        <div class="cart-item-name">${item.name}</div>
                        <button class="btn-remove" onclick="removeFromCart(${item.id})">
                            <i class="bi bi-trash"></i>
                        </button>
                    </div>
                    <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
                        <div class="qty-control">
                            <div class="qty-btn" onclick="updateQty(${item.id}, ${item.qty - 1})">
                                <i class="bi bi-dash"></i>
                            </div>
                            <input type="number" class="qty-input" value="${item.qty}" 
                                   onchange="updateQty(${item.id}, this.value)" min="1">
                            <div class="qty-btn" onclick="updateQty(${item.id}, ${item.qty + 1})">
                                <i class="bi bi-plus"></i>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="cart-item-price">
                            Rp ${formatNumber(item.price * item.qty)}
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <small style="color: var(--text-light); opacity: 0.8;">per ${item.unit}</small>
                </div>
            `).join('');
            
            // Calculate totals
            const subtotal = cart.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.price * item.qty), 0);
            let discount = 0;
            
            // Apply discount based on number of services
            const numServices = cart.length;
            if (numServices >= 5) {
                discount = subtotal * 0.15; // 15% discount for 5+ services
            } else if (numServices >= 3) {
                discount = subtotal * 0.10; // 10% discount for 3-4 services
            }
            
            const total = subtotal - discount;
            
            // Update summary
            document.getElementById('subtotal').textContent = 'Rp ' + formatNumber(subtotal);
            document.getElementById('discount').textContent = '- Rp ' + formatNumber(discount);
            document.getElementById('total').textContent = 'Rp ' + formatNumber(total);
            
            if (discount > 0) {
                document.getElementById('discountRow').style.display = 'flex';
            } else {
                document.getElementById('discountRow').style.display = 'none';
            }
            
            summary.style.display = 'block';
            comparison.style.display = 'block';
            
            // Save to localStorage
            localStorage.setItem('calculatorCart', JSON.stringify(cart));
        }
        
        // Format number
        function formatNumber(num) {
            return num.toString().replace(/\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, ".");
        }
        
        // Share to WhatsApp
        function shareToWhatsApp() {
            const subtotal = cart.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.price * item.qty), 0);
            const numServices = cart.length;
            let discount = 0;
            
            if (numServices >= 5) {
                discount = subtotal * 0.15;
            } else if (numServices >= 3) {
                discount = subtotal * 0.10;
            }
            
            const total = subtotal - discount;
            
            let message = '*ESTIMASI HARGA SITUNEO DIGITAL*\n\n';
            message += '*Layanan yang dipilih:*\n';
            cart.forEach((item, index) => {
                message += `${index + 1}. ${item.name}\n`;
                message += `   ${item.qty} ${item.unit} x Rp ${formatNumber(item.price)}\n`;
                message += `   Subtotal: Rp ${formatNumber(item.price * item.qty)}\n\n`;
            });
            
            message += `*Subtotal:* Rp ${formatNumber(subtotal)}\n`;
            if (discount > 0) {
                message += `*Diskon:* - Rp ${formatNumber(discount)}\n`;
            }
            message += `*TOTAL:* Rp ${formatNumber(total)}\n\n`;
            message += 'Saya tertarik untuk konsultasi lebih lanjut. Terima kasih!';
            
            const waUrl = '<?= $wa_link ?>?text=' + encodeURIComponent(message);
            window.open(waUrl, '_blank');
        }
        
       // Load cart from localStorage
        window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            const savedCart = localStorage.getItem('calculatorCart');
            if (savedCart) {
                cart = JSON.parse(savedCart);
                updateCart();
            }
        });
        
        // Smooth scroll
        document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
            anchor.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                const target = document.querySelector(this.getAttribute('href'));
                if (target) {
                    const offsetTop = target.offsetTop - 80;
                    window.scrollTo({
                        top: offsetTop,
                        behavior: 'smooth'
                    });
                }
            });
        });
        
        // Service card click to add
        document.querySelectorAll('.service-card').forEach(card => {
            card.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                // Don't trigger if clicking the add button
                if (!e.target.closest('button')) {
                    const serviceId = parseInt(this.getAttribute('data-id'));
                    addToCart(serviceId);
                }
            });
        });
        
        // Save estimate
        function saveEstimate() {
            const estimateData = {
                cart: cart,
                date: new Date().toISOString(),
                subtotal: cart.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.price * item.qty), 0)
            };
            
            // Save to localStorage
            const estimates = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('savedEstimates') || '[]');
            estimates.push(estimateData);
            localStorage.setItem('savedEstimates', JSON.stringify(estimates));
            
            alert('Estimasi berhasil disimpan!');
        }
        
        // Log page view
        console.log('Calculator page loaded successfully');
        console.log('Total services available: <?= count($services) ?>');
    </script>
</body>
</html>

### ASSISTANT
# üìã ANALISIS & PERBAIKAN FILE calculator.php

Saya telah menganalisis file calculator.php yang Anda kirimkan. Berikut adalah analisis lengkap dan perbaikan yang diperlukan:

## üîç ANALISIS FILE

### Status Umum
- File sudah memiliki struktur yang baik dengan desain modern
- Sudah mendukung multi-bahasa (ID/EN)
- Menggunakan AOS animation untuk efek scroll
- Sudah responsive untuk mobile
- Fitur kalkulator harga interaktif sudah berfungsi dengan baik

### ‚ùå MASALAH YANG DITEMUKAN

1. **Nomor WhatsApp tidak konsisten**
   - File ini menggunakan `628170404594`
   - Seharusnya `6283173868915` sesuai data perusahaan

2. **Email tidak konsisten**
   - Footer menggunakan `info@situneo.my.id`
   - Seharusnya `vins@situneo.my.id` (utama) dan `support@situneo.my.id` (support)

## üõ†Ô∏è PERBAIKAN YANG DIPERLUKAN

### 1. Perbaiki Nomor WhatsApp (Line 35)

```php
// WhatsApp Number
$wa_number = '6283173868915'; // DARI 628170404594
$wa_link = "https://wa.me/{$wa_number}";
```

### 2. Perbaiki Email di Footer (Line 730)

```php
    <a href="mailto:vins@situneo.my.id" style="color: var(--text-light);">vins@situneo.my.id</a>
</li>
```

### 3. Perbaiki Nomor WhatsApp di Footer (Line 735)


### 3. Tambahkan Fitur Export ke PDF

```javascript
// Export to PDF function
function exportToPDF() {
    const { jsPDF } = window.jspdf;
    const doc = new jsPDF();
    
    // Add title
    doc.setFontSize(20);
    doc.text('ESTIMASI HARGA SITUNEO DIGITAL', 105, 20, { align: 'center' });
    
    // Add date
    doc.setFontSize(12);
    doc.text(`Tanggal: ${new Date().toLocaleDateString('id-ID')}`, 20, 35);
    
    // Add services
    let yPosition = 50;
    doc.setFontSize(14);
    doc.text('Layanan yang dipilih:', 20, yPosition);
    yPosition += 10;
    
    doc.setFontSize(12);
    cart.forEach((item, index) => {
        doc.text(`${index + 1}. ${item.name}`, 20, yPosition);
        yPosition += 7;
        doc.text(`   ${item.qty} ${item.unit} x Rp ${formatNumber(item.price)}`, 25, yPosition);
        yPosition += 7;
        doc.text(`   Subtotal: Rp ${formatNumber(item.price * item.qty)}`, 25, yPosition);
        yPosition += 10;
    });
    
    // Add total
    const subtotal = cart.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.price * item.qty), 0);
    const numServices = cart.length;
    let discount = 0;
    
    if (numServices >= 5) {
        discount = subtotal * 0.15;
    } else if (numServices >= 3) {
        discount = subtotal * 0.10;
    }
    
    const total = subtotal - discount;
    
    yPosition += 10;
    doc.text(`Subtotal: Rp ${formatNumber(subtotal)}`, 20, yPosition);
    yPosition += 7;
    if (discount > 0) {
        doc.text(`Diskon: - Rp ${formatNumber(discount)}`, 20, yPosition);
        yPosition += 7;
    }
    doc.setFontSize(14);
    doc.text(`TOTAL: Rp ${formatNumber(total)}`, 20, yPosition);
    
    // Save the PDF
    doc.save('estimasi-harga-situneo.pdf');
}
```

### 4. Tambahkan Tombol Export ke PDF

```html
<button class="btn-outline-gold mb-2" onclick="exportToPDF()">
    <i class="bi bi-file-pdf"></i> Export PDF
</button>
```

### 5. Tambahkan Tracking Analytics

```javascript
// Track calculator usage
function trackCalculatorUsage(action, data) {
    // Send to Google Analytics 4
    gtag('event', action, {
        'event_category': 'Calculator',
        'event_label': data,
        'value': data
    });
}

// Track when service is added to cart
function addToCart(serviceId) {
    // ... existing code ...
    
    // Track this action
    trackCalculatorUsage('add_to_cart', serviceId);
}

// Track when calculation is shared
function shareToWhatsApp() {
    // ... existing code ...
    
    // Track this action
    trackCalculatorUsage('share_to_whatsapp', cart.length);
}
```

    <!-- Bootstrap JS -->
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
    
    <!-- AOS Animation -->
    <script src="https://unpkg.com/aos@2.3.1/dist/aos.js"></script>
    
    <!-- Custom Scripts -->
    <script>
        // Initialize AOS
        AOS.init({
            duration: 800,
            once: true,
            offset: 100
        });
        
        // Navbar scroll effect
        window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
            const navbar = document.querySelector('.navbar');
            if (window.scrollY > 50) {
                navbar.classList.add('scrolled');
            } else {
                navbar.classList.remove('scrolled');
            }
        });
        
        // Form submission handling
        const contactForm = document.getElementById('contactForm');
        const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submitBtn');
        
        contactForm.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            // Show loading state
            submitBtn.disabled = true;
            submitBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="bi bi-hourglass-split"></i> <?= $t['form_sending'] ?>';
            
            // Form will submit normally to PHP
            // The disabled state and loading text provide user feedback
        });
        
        // Auto-hide alerts after 5 seconds
        const alerts = document.querySelectorAll('.alert-custom');
        alerts.forEach(alert => {
            setTimeout(() => {
                alert.style.opacity = '0';
                alert.style.transform = 'translateY(-20px)';
                setTimeout(() => alert.remove(), 500);
            }, 5000);
        });
        
        // Smooth scroll
        document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
            anchor.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                const target = document.querySelector(this.getAttribute('href'));
                if (target) {
                    const offsetTop = target.offsetTop - 80;
                    window.scrollTo({
                        top: offsetTop,
                        behavior: 'smooth'
                    });
                }
            });
        });
        
        // Form validation enhancement
        const formInputs = contactForm.querySelectorAll('input, textarea, select');
        formInputs.forEach(input => {
            input.addEventListener('blur', function() {
                if (this.hasAttribute('required') && !this.value.trim()) {
                    this.style.borderColor = '#FF0000';
                } else {
                    this.style.borderColor = 'rgba(255,180,0,0.3)';
                }
            });
            
            input.addEventListener('focus', function() {
                this.style.borderColor = 'var(--gold)';
            });
        });
        
        // Log page view
        console.log('Contact page loaded successfully');
        console.log('Ready to receive messages');
    </script>
</body>
</html>

   ```javascript
   // Check if currently open
   function checkOperatingHours() {
       const now = new Date();
       const day = now.getDay(); // 0 = Sunday, 1 = Monday, etc.
       const hour = now.getHours();
       
       let isOpen = false;
       
       if (day >= 1 && day <= 5) { // Monday - Friday
           isOpen = hour >= 9 && hour < 18;
       } else if (day === 0 || day === 6) { // Saturday - Sunday
           isOpen = hour >= 10 && hour < 16;
       }
       
       const statusElement = document.getElementById('status-hours');
       if (isOpen) {
           statusElement.innerHTML = '<i class="bi bi-circle-fill text-success"></i> Sedang Buka';
       } else {
           statusElement.innerHTML = '<i class="bi bi-circle-fill text-danger"></i> Sedang Tutup';
       }
   }
   ```

# ========================================
# SITUNEO DIGITAL - Apache Configuration
# .htaccess for URL rewriting & security
# ========================================

# Enable Rewrite Engine
<IfModule mod_rewrite.c>
    RewriteEngine On
    RewriteBase /
    
    # Force HTTPS (uncomment in production)
    # RewriteCond %{HTTPS} off
    # RewriteRule ^(.*)$ https://%{HTTP_HOST}%{REQUEST_URI} [L,R=301]
    
    # Remove www (optional)
    # RewriteCond %{HTTP_HOST} ^www\.(.*)$ [NC]
    # RewriteRule ^(.*)$ https://%1/$1 [R=301,L]
    
    # Custom 404 Error Page
    ErrorDocument 404 /404.php
    
    # Protect sensitive files
    <FilesMatch "^(config\.php|\.env|\.git|\.htaccess|composer\.(json|lock))$">
        Order allow,deny
        Deny from all
    </FilesMatch>
    
    # Block access to includes directory
    RewriteRule ^includes/ - [F,L]
    
    # Block access to uploads directory browsing (but allow file access)
    Options -Indexes
</IfModule>

# Security Headers
<IfModule mod_headers.c>
    # Prevent clickjacking
    Header always set X-Frame-Options "SAMEORIGIN"
    
    # XSS Protection
    Header always set X-XSS-Protection "1; mode=block"
    
    # Prevent MIME sniffing
    Header always set X-Content-Type-Options "nosniff"
    
    # Referrer Policy
    Header always set Referrer-Policy "strict-origin-when-cross-origin"
    
    # Remove PHP version
    Header unset X-Powered-By
</IfModule>

# PHP Settings
<IfModule mod_php7.c>
    # Increase upload limits
    php_value upload_max_filesize 10M
    php_value post_max_size 12M
    php_value max_execution_time 300
    php_value max_input_time 300
    
    # Error handling (disable in production)
    php_flag display_errors Off
    php_flag display_startup_errors Off
    php_value error_reporting 0
    
    # Hide PHP version
    php_flag expose_php Off
    
    # Session security
    php_value session.cookie_httponly 1
    php_value session.cookie_secure 0
    php_value session.use_strict_mode 1
</IfModule>

# Compression
<IfModule mod_deflate.c>
    AddOutputFilterByType DEFLATE text/html text/plain text/xml text/css text/javascript application/javascript application/json
</IfModule>

# Browser Caching
<IfModule mod_expires.c>
    ExpiresActive On
    
    # Images
    ExpiresByType image/jpeg "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType image/png "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType image/gif "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType image/webp "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType image/svg+xml "access plus 1 year"
    
    # CSS and JavaScript
    ExpiresByType text/css "access plus 1 month"
    ExpiresByType application/javascript "access plus 1 month"
    
    # Fonts
    ExpiresByType font/woff2 "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType font/woff "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType font/ttf "access plus 1 year"
</IfModule>

# File Upload Protection
<FilesMatch "\.(php|php3|php4|php5|phtml)$">
    <IfModule mod_rewrite.c>
        RewriteEngine On
        RewriteCond %{REQUEST_FILENAME} uploads/
        RewriteRule .* - [F,L]
    </IfModule>
</FilesMatch>

# Protect against SQL injection
<IfModule mod_rewrite.c>
    RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} (\<|%3C).*script.*(\>|%3E) [NC,OR]
    RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} GLOBALS(=|\[|\%[0-9A-Z]{0,2}) [OR]
    RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} _REQUEST(=|\[|\%[0-9A-Z]{0,2})
    RewriteRule ^(.*)$ - [F,L]
</IfModule>

# Prevent directory listing
Options -Indexes

# Default charset
AddDefaultCharset UTF-8

# üìã ANALISIS & REKOMENDASI .htaccess UNTUK SITUNEO DIGITAL

Saya telah menganalisis file .htaccess yang Anda berikan. Berikut adalah analisis lengkap dan rekomendasi untuk pengoptimalan keamanan dan performa website Situneo Digital:

## üîç ANALISIS FILE .htaccess

### Status Umum
- File sudah memiliki konfigurasi dasar yang baik
- Sudah mengaktifkan URL rewriting
- Sudah memiliki beberapa pengaturan keamanan dasar
- Sudah mengaktifkan kompresi dan browser caching

### ‚úÖ ASPEK YANG SUDAH BAIK

1. **URL Rewriting** - Sudah diaktifkan dengan benar
2. **Error Document** - Custom 404 page sudah dikonfigurasi
3. **File Protection** - Perlindungan untuk file sensitif sudah ada
4. **Security Headers** - Beberapa security header sudah diatur
5. **PHP Settings** - Pengaturan PHP yang tepat untuk produksi
6. **Compression** - Gzip compression sudah diaktifkan
7. **Browser Caching** - Cache expiration untuk berbagai tipe file
8. **SQL Injection Protection** - Dasar perlindungan sudah ada

## üõ†Ô∏è REKOMENDASI PENINGKATAN

### 1. Aktifkan HTTPS di Produksi

```apache
# Force HTTPS (uncomment in production)
RewriteCond %{HTTPS} off
RewriteRule ^(.*)$ https://%{HTTP_HOST}%{REQUEST_URI} [L,R=301]
```

### 2. Tambahkan URL Rewriting untuk Clean URLs

```apache
# Clean URLs for pages
RewriteRule ^about$ about.php [L]
RewriteRule ^services$ services.php [L]
RewriteRule ^portfolio$ portfolio.php [L]
RewriteRule ^pricing$ pricing.php [L]
RewriteRule ^contact$ contact.php [L]
RewriteRule ^calculator$ calculator.php [L]

# Clean URLs for auth
RewriteRule ^login$ auth/login.php [L]
RewriteRule ^register$ auth/register.php [L]
RewriteRule ^logout$ auth/logout.php [L]

# Clean URLs for dashboard
RewriteRule ^dashboard$ client/index.php [L]
RewriteRule ^admin$ admin/index.php [L]
RewriteRule ^freelancer$ freelance/index.php [L]

# API endpoints
RewriteRule ^api/(.*)$ api/$1.php [L]
```

### 3. Tingkatkan Keamanan dengan Tambahan Headers

```apache
# Additional Security Headers
Header always set Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' https://cdn.jsdelivr.net https://www.google.com https://www.gstatic.com; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' https://cdn.jsdelivr.net https://fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' https://fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data: https:; connect-src 'self' https://wa.me; frame-src https://www.google.com"
Header always set Permissions-Policy "geolocation=(), microphone=(), camera=()"
Header always set Strict-Transport-Security "max-age=31536000; includeSubDomains"
```

### 4. Tambahkan Perlindungan Lebih Lanjut

```apache
# Block suspicious user agents
RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^-?$ [OR]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Ww]eb[Bb]andit.*$ [OR]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Aa]tomic.*[Hh]arvester.*$ [OR]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Aa]tomic.*[Ee]mail.*[Hh]arvester.*$ [OR]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Ee]mail.*[Cc]ollector.*$ [OR]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Ss]earch.*[Ee]ngine.*$ [OR]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Ss]pider.*$ [OR]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Bb]ot.*$ [OR]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Ss]canner.*$ [OR]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Cc]rawler.*$ [OR]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Hh]arvester.*$ [OR]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Dd]igger.*$ [OR]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Ss]ucker.*$
RewriteRule ^.* - [F,L]

# Block bad referrers
RewriteCond %{HTTP_REFERER} ^https?://.*[Bb]ad[Rr]eferrer.*$ [NC,OR]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_REFERER} ^https?://.*[Ss]pam.*[Ss]ite.*$ [NC,OR]
RewriteCond %{HTTP_REFERER} ^https?://.*[Pp]orn.*$ [NC]
RewriteRule ^.* - [F,L]

# Prevent access to debug logs
<FilesMatch "\.(log|debug)$">
    Order allow,deny
    Deny from all
</FilesMatch>

# Limit request size to prevent DoS attacks
LimitRequestBody 10485760
```

### 5. Optimasi Performa Tambahan

```apache
# Enable HTTP/2
<IfModule mod_http2.c>
    Protocols h2 h2c http/1.1
</IfModule>

# Preload critical resources
<FilesMatch "\.(css|js)$">
    Header set Link "</assets/css/main.css>; rel=preload; as=style"
    Header set Link "</assets/js/main.js>; rel=preload; as=script"
</FilesMatch>

# Optimize images
<IfModule mod_rewrite.c>
    RewriteCond %{REQUEST_FILENAME} \.(jpe?g|png|gif)$
    RewriteCond %{REQUEST_FILENAME} !-f
    RewriteRule ^(.*)$ /image.php?src=$1 [L]
</IfModule>
```

### 6. Konfigurasi untuk Multi-Bahasa

```apache
# Language detection and redirection
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/$ [NC]
RewriteCond %{HTTP:Accept-Language} (id) [NC]
RewriteRule ^$ /?lang=id [L,R=302]

RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/$ [NC]
RewriteCond %{HTTP:Accept-Language} !(id) [NC]
RewriteRule ^$ /?lang=en [L,R=302]
```

### 7. Konfigurasi untuk API Endpoints

```apache
# API rate limiting
<IfModule mod_rewrite.c>
    RewriteCond %{REQUEST_METHOD} POST
    RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/api/
    RewriteCond %{REMOTE_ADDR} ^(127\.0\.0\.1|::1)$ [OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP:X-API-Key} ^your-secret-api-key$
    RewriteRule ^(.*)$ - [L]
    
    # Block API requests without proper authentication
    RewriteCond %{REQUEST_METHOD} POST
    RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/api/
    RewriteRule ^(.*)$ - [F,L]
</IfModule>
```

## üìä VERSI LENGKAP .htaccess YANG DIREKOMENDASIKAN

```apache
# ========================================
# SITUNEO DIGITAL - Apache Configuration
# .htaccess for URL rewriting & security
# ========================================

# Enable Rewrite Engine
<IfModule mod_rewrite.c>
    RewriteEngine On
    RewriteBase /
    
    # Force HTTPS (uncomment in production)
    RewriteCond %{HTTPS} off
    RewriteRule ^(.*)$ https://%{HTTP_HOST}%{REQUEST_URI} [L,R=301]
    
    # Remove www (optional)
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_HOST} ^www\.(.*)$ [NC]
    RewriteRule ^(.*)$ https://%1/$1 [R=301,L]
    
    # Custom 404 Error Page
    ErrorDocument 404 /404.php
    
    # Clean URLs for pages
    RewriteRule ^about$ about.php [L]
    RewriteRule ^services$ services.php [L]
    RewriteRule ^portfolio$ portfolio.php [L]
    RewriteRule ^pricing$ pricing.php [L]
    RewriteRule ^contact$ contact.php [L]
    RewriteRule ^calculator$ calculator.php [L]
    
    # Clean URLs for auth
    RewriteRule ^login$ auth/login.php [L]
    RewriteRule ^register$ auth/register.php [L]
    RewriteRule ^logout$ auth/logout.php [L]
    
    # Clean URLs for dashboard
    RewriteRule ^dashboard$ client/index.php [L]
    RewriteRule ^admin$ admin/index.php [L]
    RewriteRule ^freelancer$ freelance/index.php [L]
    
    # API endpoints
    RewriteRule ^api/(.*)$ api/$1.php [L]
    
    # Language detection and redirection
    RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/$ [NC]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP:Accept-Language} (id) [NC]
    RewriteRule ^$ /?lang=id [L,R=302]
    
    RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/$ [NC]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP:Accept-Language} !(id) [NC]
    RewriteRule ^$ /?lang=en [L,R=302]
    
    # Protect sensitive files
    <FilesMatch "^(config\.php|\.env|\.git|\.htaccess|composer\.(json|lock))$">
        Order allow,deny
        Deny from all
    </FilesMatch>
    
    # Block access to includes directory
    RewriteRule ^includes/ - [F,L]
    
    # Block access to uploads directory browsing (but allow file access)
    Options -Indexes
    
    # Block suspicious user agents
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^-?$ [OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Ww]eb[Bb]andit.*$ [OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Aa]tomic.*[Hh]arvester.*$ [OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Aa]tomic.*[Ee]mail.*[Hh]arvester.*$ [OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Ee]mail.*[Cc]ollector.*$ [OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Ss]earch.*[Ee]ngine.*$ [OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Ss]pider.*$ [OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Bb]ot.*$ [OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Ss]canner.*$ [OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Cc]rawler.*$ [OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Hh]arvester.*$ [OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Dd]igger.*$ [OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_USER_AGENT} ^.*[Ss]ucker.*$
    RewriteRule ^.* - [F,L]
    
    # Block bad referrers
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_REFERER} ^https?://.*[Bb]ad[Rr]eferrer.*$ [NC,OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_REFERER} ^https?://.*[Ss]pam.*[Ss]ite.*$ [NC,OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP_REFERER} ^https?://.*[Pp]orn.*$ [NC]
    RewriteRule ^.* - [F,L]
    
    # API rate limiting
    RewriteCond %{REQUEST_METHOD} POST
    RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/api/
    RewriteCond %{REMOTE_ADDR} ^(127\.0\.0\.1|::1)$ [OR]
    RewriteCond %{HTTP:X-API-Key} ^your-secret-api-key$
    RewriteRule ^(.*)$ - [L]
    
    # Block API requests without proper authentication
    RewriteCond %{REQUEST_METHOD} POST
    RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} ^/api/
    RewriteRule ^(.*)$ - [F,L]
    
    # Protect against SQL injection
    RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} (\<|%3C).*script.*(\>|%3E) [NC,OR]
    RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} GLOBALS(=|\[|\%[0-9A-Z]{0,2}) [OR]
    RewriteCond %{QUERY_STRING} _REQUEST(=|\[|\%[0-9A-Z]{0,2})
    RewriteRule ^(.*)$ - [F,L]
</IfModule>

# Security Headers
<IfModule mod_headers.c>
    # Prevent clickjacking
    Header always set X-Frame-Options "SAMEORIGIN"
    
    # XSS Protection
    Header always set X-XSS-Protection "1; mode=block"
    
    # Prevent MIME sniffing
    Header always set X-Content-Type-Options "nosniff"
    
    # Referrer Policy
    Header always set Referrer-Policy "strict-origin-when-cross-origin"
    
    # Content Security Policy
    Header always set Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' https://cdn.jsdelivr.net https://www.google.com https://www.gstatic.com; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' https://cdn.jsdelivr.net https://fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' https://fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data: https:; connect-src 'self' https://wa.me; frame-src https://www.google.com"
    
    # Permissions Policy
    Header always set Permissions-Policy "geolocation=(), microphone=(), camera=()"
    
    # HSTS (uncomment when HTTPS is active)
    Header always set Strict-Transport-Security "max-age=31536000; includeSubDomains"
    
    # Remove PHP version
    Header unset X-Powered-By
</IfModule>

# PHP Settings
<IfModule mod_php7.c>
    # Increase upload limits
    php_value upload_max_filesize 10M
    php_value post_max_size 12M
    php_value max_execution_time 300
    php_value max_input_time 300
    
    # Error handling (disable in production)
    php_flag display_errors Off
    php_flag display_startup_errors Off
    php_value error_reporting 0
    
    # Hide PHP version
    php_flag expose_php Off
    
    # Session security
    php_value session.cookie_httponly 1
    php_value session.cookie_secure 1
    php_value session.use_strict_mode 1
</IfModule>

# Enable HTTP/2
<IfModule mod_http2.c>
    Protocols h2 h2c http/1.1
</IfModule>

# Compression
<IfModule mod_deflate.c>
    AddOutputFilterByType DEFLATE text/html text/plain text/xml text/css text/javascript application/javascript application/json
</IfModule>

# Browser Caching
<IfModule mod_expires.c>
    ExpiresActive On
    
    # Images
    ExpiresByType image/jpeg "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType image/png "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType image/gif "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType image/webp "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType image/svg+xml "access plus 1 year"
    
    # CSS and JavaScript
    ExpiresByType text/css "access plus 1 month"
    ExpiresByType application/javascript "access plus 1 month"
    
    # Fonts
    ExpiresByType font/woff2 "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType font/woff "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType font/ttf "access plus 1 year"
</IfModule>

# File Upload Protection
<FilesMatch "\.(php|php3|php4|php5|phtml)$">
    <IfModule mod_rewrite.c>
        RewriteEngine On
        RewriteCond %{REQUEST_FILENAME} uploads/
        RewriteRule .* - [F,L]
    </IfModule>
</FilesMatch>

# Prevent access to debug logs
<FilesMatch "\.(log|debug)$">
    Order allow,deny
    Deny from all
</FilesMatch>

# Limit request size to prevent DoS attacks
LimitRequestBody 10485760

# Prevent directory listing
Options -Indexes

# Default charset
AddDefaultCharset UTF-8
```

## üéØ IMPLEMENTASI REKOMENDASI

1. **Backup file .htaccess existing** sebelum melakukan perubahan
2. **Implementasi bertahap** - tambahkan konfigurasi satu per satu dan test
3. **Monitor error logs** setelah implementasi untuk memastikan tidak ada masalah
4. **Test keamanan** dengan tools seperti SecurityHeaders.com untuk memverifikasi headers
5. **Test performa** dengan GTmetrix atau PageSpeed Insights untuk memverifikasi optimasi

## ‚úÖ STATUS SETELAH IMPLEMENTASI

Setelah menerapkan rekomendasi di atas:
- ‚úÖ Keamanan website meningkat secara signifikan
- ‚úÖ Performa loading halaman lebih optimal
- ‚úÖ URL lebih bersih dan SEO-friendly
- ‚úÖ Perlindungan dari serangan umum
- ‚úÖ Konfigurasi yang sesuai untuk production environment

File .htaccess yang diperbarui akan membantu Situneo Digital memiliki website yang lebih aman, cepat, dan optimal untuk mesin pencari.

Apakah Anda ingin saya membantu dengan aspek lain dari konfigurasi server atau ada pertanyaan tentang implementasi .htaccess ini?

    <!-- JavaScript Libraries -->
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.3/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
    <script src="https://unpkg.com/aos@2.3.1/dist/aos.js"></script>
    
    <script>
        // Initialize AOS
        AOS.init({
            duration: 1000,
            once: true,
            offset: 100
        });
        
        // Loading Screen
        window.addEventListener('load', function() {
            setTimeout(function() {
                document.getElementById('loadingScreen').classList.add('hidden');
            }, 1500);
        });
        
        // Auto Show Demo Modal after 10 seconds
        setTimeout(function() {
            var demoModal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('demoModal'));
            demoModal.show();
        }, 10000); // 10 detik
        
        // Navbar Scroll Effect
        window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
            const navbar = document.querySelector('.navbar-premium');
            const backToTop = document.getElementById('backToTop');
            
            if (window.scrollY > 100) {
                navbar.classList.add('scrolled');
                backToTop.style.display = 'block';
            } else {
                navbar.classList.remove('scrolled');
                backToTop.style.display = 'none';
            }
        });
        
        // Back to Top
        document.getElementById('backToTop').addEventListener('click', function() {
            window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
        });
        
        // Smooth Scroll
        document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
            anchor.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                const href = this.getAttribute('href');
                if (href !== '#' && href !== '#demoModal') {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    const target = document.querySelector(href);
                    if (target) {
                        const offset = 100;
                        const targetPosition = target.offsetTop - offset;
                        window.scrollTo({
                            top: targetPosition,
                            behavior: 'smooth'
                        });
                    }
                }
            });
        });
        
        // Counter Animation
        function animateCounter() {
            const counters = document.querySelectorAll('.counter');
            counters.forEach(counter => {
                const target = parseInt(counter.getAttribute('data-target'));
                const duration = 2000;
                const step = target / (duration / 16);
                let current = 0;
                
                const updateCounter = () => {
                    current += step;
                    if (current < target) {
                        counter.textContent = Math.floor(current);
                        requestAnimationFrame(updateCounter);
                    } else {
                        counter.textContent = target;
                    }
                };
                
                updateCounter();
            });
        }
        
        const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
            entries.forEach(entry => {
                if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                    animateCounter();
                    observer.unobserve(entry.target);
                }
            });
        });
        
        const aboutSection = document.querySelector('#about');
        if (aboutSection) observer.observe(aboutSection);
        
        // Order Notification System (LEFT BOTTOM)
        const orderNotifications = [
            { name: 'Budi Santoso', order: 'Website Toko Online', time: '2 menit yang lalu' },
            { name: 'Sarah Wijaya', order: 'Website Company Profile', time: '5 menit yang lalu' },
            { name: 'Dr. Ahmad', order: 'Website Klinik', time: '8 menit yang lalu' },
            { name: 'Rina Kusuma', order: 'Website Restoran', time: '12 menit yang lalu' },
            { name: 'Hendro', order: 'Website Portfolio', time: '15 menit yang lalu' },
            { name: 'Lisa Permata', order: 'Landing Page', time: '20 menit yang lalu' },
            { name: 'Dedi Kurniawan', order: 'Toko Online', time: '25 menit yang lalu' },
            { name: 'Maya Sari', order: 'Website Spa', time: '30 menit yang lalu' }
        ];
        
        function showOrderNotification() {
            const notification = document.getElementById('orderNotification');
            const randomNotif = orderNotifications[Math.floor(Math.random() * orderNotifications.length)];
            
            // Update content
            document.getElementById('notifName').textContent = randomNotif.name;
            document.getElementById('notifOrder').textContent = 'Baru pesan ' + randomNotif.order;
            document.getElementById('notifTime').textContent = randomNotif.time;
            document.getElementById('notifAvatar').src = 'https://ui-avatars.com/api/?name=' + encodeURIComponent(randomNotif.name) + '&background=FFB400&color=0F3057&size=100';
            
            // Show notification
            notification.classList.add('show');
            notification.classList.remove('hide');
            
            // Auto hide after 10 seconds
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.classList.add('hide');
                setTimeout(() => {
                    notification.classList.remove('show');
                    notification.classList.remove('hide');
                }, 500);
            }, 10000);
        }
        
        function closeNotification() {
            const notification = document.getElementById('orderNotification');
            notification.classList.add('hide');
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.classList.remove('show');
                notification.classList.remove('hide');
            }, 500);
        }
        
        // Show first notification after 5 seconds, then every 30 seconds
        setTimeout(showOrderNotification, 5000);
        setInterval(showOrderNotification, 30000);
        
        // Network Background Animation
        const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
        const networkBg = document.getElementById('networkBg');
        networkBg.appendChild(canvas);
        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
        
        canvas.width = window.innerWidth;
        canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
        
        const particles = [];
        const particleCount = 80;
        
        class Particle {
            constructor() {
                this.x = Math.random() * canvas.width;
                this.y = Math.random() * canvas.height;
                this.vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;
                this.vy = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;
                this.radius = Math.random() * 2 + 1;
            }
            
            update() {
                this.x += this.vx;
                this.y += this.vy;
                
                if (this.x < 0 || this.x > canvas.width) this.vx *= -1;
                if (this.y < 0 || this.y > canvas.height) this.vy *= -1;
            }
            
            draw() {
                ctx.beginPath();
                ctx.arc(this.x, this.y, this.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
                ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255, 180, 0, 0.5)';
                ctx.fill();
            }
        }
        
        for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
            particles.push(new Particle());
        }
        
        function connectParticles() {
            for (let i = 0; i < particles.length; i++) {
                for (let j = i + 1; j < particles.length; j++) {
                    const dx = particles[i].x - particles[j].x;
                    const dy = particles[i].y - particles[j].y;
                    const distance = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
                    
                    if (distance < 150) {
                        ctx.beginPath();
                        ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(255, 180, 0, ${0.2 * (1 - distance / 150)})`;
                        ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
                        ctx.moveTo(particles[i].x, particles[i].y);
                        ctx.lineTo(particles[j].x, particles[j].y);
                        ctx.stroke();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        function animate() {
            ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
            
            particles.forEach(particle => {
                particle.update();
                particle.draw();
            });
            
            connectParticles();
            requestAnimationFrame(animate);
        }
        
        animate();
        
        window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
            canvas.width = window.innerWidth;
            canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

### 3. Tambahkan Tracking Analytics

```javascript
// Google Analytics 4 Configuration
window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
function gtag(){dataLayer.push(arguments);}
gtag('js', new Date());
gtag('config', 'GA_MEASUREMENT_ID', {
    'custom_map': {'custom_parameter_1': 'page_category'}
});

// Track CTA Button Clicks
document.querySelectorAll('.btn-gold, .btn-outline-warning, .btn-success').forEach(button => {
    button.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const buttonText = this.textContent.trim();
        gtag('event', 'cta_click', {
            'event_category': 'Engagement',
            'event_label': buttonText,
            'value': 1
        });
    });
});

// Track Demo Modal Views
const demoModal = document.getElementById('demoModal');
demoModal.addEventListener('shown.bs.modal', function () {
    gtag('event', 'view_modal', {
        'event_category': 'Engagement',
        'event_label': 'Demo Modal',
        'value': 1
    });
});

// Track Order Notification Views
function trackNotificationView() {
    gtag('event', 'view_notification', {
        'event_category': 'Engagement',
        'event_label': 'Order Notification',
        'value': 1
    });
}
```

### 4. Tambahkan Fitur Lead Capture

```javascript
// Email Lead Capture for Demo Request
function captureEmailForDemo(email, name) {
    fetch('api/capture-lead.php', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({
            email: email,
            name: name,
            source: 'homepage_demo_modal',
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        })
    })
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(data => {
        if (data.success) {
            console.log('Lead captured successfully');
            // Trigger WhatsApp or redirect to registration
            window.open('https://wa.me/6283173868915?text=Halo%20Situneo,%20saya%20mau%20request%20FREE%20DEMO', '_blank');
        }
    })
    .catch(error => {
        console.error('Error capturing lead:', error);
        // Fallback to direct WhatsApp
        window.open('https://wa.me/6283173868915?text=Halo%20Situneo,%20saya%20mau%20request%20FREE%20DEMO', '_blank');
    });
}

// Add email capture form to demo modal
// Add this HTML to the modal body
/*
<div class="email-capture-form mt-3">
    <div class="input-group">
        <input type="email" class="form-control" id="demoEmail" placeholder="Email Anda">
        <input type="text" class="form-control" id="demoName" placeholder="Nama Anda">
        <button class="btn btn-gold" onclick="captureEmailForDemo(document.getElementById('demoEmail').value, document.getElementById('demoName').value)">
            Request Demo
        </button>
    </div>
</div>
*/
```

### 5. Tambahkan Fitur A/B Testing

```javascript
// A/B Testing for Headlines
const headlines = [
    'Bikin Website Profesional Cuma Rp 350rb/Halaman',
    'Website Profesional Mulai Rp 350rb - FREE DEMO 24 Jam',
    'Rp 350rb/Halaman - Website Termurah Se-Indonesia'
];

function getRandomHeadline() {
    return headlines[Math.floor(Math.random() * headlines.length)];
}

// Set random headline on page load
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const heroTitle = document.querySelector('.hero-title');
    if (heroTitle) {
        const selectedHeadline = getRandomHeadline();
        heroTitle.textContent = selectedHeadline;
        
        // Track which headline was shown
        gtag('event', 'view_headline', {
            'event_category': 'A/B Test',
            'event_label': selectedHeadline,
            'value': 1
        });
    }
});
```

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Struktur dari tabel `reviews`
--

CREATE TABLE `reviews` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `project_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `client_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `freelancer_id` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `rating` int(11) NOT NULL CHECK (`rating` between 1 and 5),
  `review_text` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_approved` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 0,
  `is_featured` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 0,
  `approved_by` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `approved_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp(),
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp() ON UPDATE current_timestamp()
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

--
-- Struktur dari tabel `users`
--

CREATE TABLE `users` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `password` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `role` enum('admin','client','freelancer') NOT NULL,
  `is_verified` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 0,
  `verification_token` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `reset_token` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `reset_token_expires` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `is_active` tinyint(1) DEFAULT 1,
  `last_login` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp(),
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp() ON UPDATE current_timestamp()
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

### ASSISTANT
# üìã ANALISIS LENGKAP DATABASE SITUNEO DIGITAL

Saya telah menganalisis struktur database yang Anda berikan. Berikut adalah analisis lengkap dan rekomendasi untuk optimasi:

## üîç ANALISIS DATABASE

### Status Umum
- Database sudah memiliki struktur yang sangat baik dengan 17 tabel utama
- Sudah mendukung multi-bahasa (ID/EN) untuk konten
- Sudah memiliki relasi yang tepat antar tabel dengan foreign key constraints
- Sudah memiliki indexing yang baik untuk performa query
- Sudah memiliki data awal untuk tabel-tabel penting (services, packages, team members, dll.)

### ‚úÖ ASPEK YANG SUDAH SANGAT BAIK

1. **Struktur Tabel** - Desain database sudah normalized dengan baik
2. **Relasi Antar Tabel** - Foreign key constraints sudah tepat
3. **Indexing** - Index sudah didefinisikan untuk kolom-kolom krusial
4. **Multi-bahasa** - Sudah mendukung konten dalam 2 bahasa
5. **Data Awal** - Sudah ada sample data untuk tabel-tabel penting
6. **Security** - Password sudah di-hash dengan bcrypt
7. **Audit Trail** - Tabel activity_logs untuk tracking aktivitas

## üõ†Ô∏è REKOMENDASI OPTIMASI

### 1. Tambahkan Trigger untuk Auto-Update

```sql
-- Trigger untuk auto-update total_orders di tabel packages
DELIMITER //
CREATE TRIGGER update_package_total_orders
AFTER INSERT ON order_items
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
    UPDATE packages 
    SET total_orders = total_orders + 1 
    WHERE id = NEW.service_id;
END//
DELIMITER ;

-- Trigger untuk auto-update total_orders di tabel services
DELIMITER //
CREATE TRIGGER update_service_total_orders
AFTER INSERT ON order_items
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
    UPDATE services 
    SET total_orders = total_orders + 1 
    WHERE id = NEW.service_id;
END//
DELIMITER ;
```

### 2. Tambahkan View untuk Query Kompleks

```sql
-- View untuk dashboard admin
CREATE VIEW admin_dashboard AS
SELECT 
    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM users WHERE role = 'client') AS total_clients,
    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM users WHERE role = 'freelancer') AS total_freelancers,
    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM orders WHERE status = 'completed') AS completed_orders,
    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM orders WHERE status = 'pending') AS pending_orders,
    (SELECT SUM(final_amount) FROM orders WHERE status = 'completed') AS total_revenue,
    (SELECT AVG(rating) FROM reviews) AS average_rating;

-- View untuk statistik layanan populer
CREATE VIEW popular_services AS
SELECT 
    s.id, s.name_en, s.name_id, s.base_price,
    COUNT(oi.id) AS order_count,
    SUM(oi.subtotal) AS total_revenue
FROM services s
LEFT JOIN order_items oi ON s.id = oi.service_id
GROUP BY s.id
ORDER BY order_count DESC;
```

### 3. Tambahkan Stored Procedure untuk Operasi Kompleks

```sql
-- Stored procedure untuk membuat order baru
DELIMITER //
CREATE PROCEDURE create_new_order(
    IN p_client_id INT,
    IN p_order_type VARCHAR(20),
    IN p_package_id INT,
    IN p_final_amount DECIMAL(15,2),
    IN p_notes TEXT
)
BEGIN
    DECLARE v_order_number VARCHAR(50);
    DECLARE v_order_id INT;
    
    -- Generate order number
    SET v_order_number = CONCAT('ORD-', DATE_FORMAT(NOW(), '%Y%m%d'), '-', LPAD(FLOOR(RAND() * 1000), 4, '0'));
    
    -- Insert order
    INSERT INTO orders (order_number, client_id, order_type, package_id, final_amount, notes)
    VALUES (v_order_number, p_client_id, p_order_type, p_package_id, p_final_amount, p_notes);
    
    -- Get order ID
    SET v_order_id = LAST_INSERT_ID();
    
    -- Create invoice
    INSERT INTO invoices (invoice_number, order_id, client_id, issue_date, due_date, total_amount)
    VALUES (
        CONCAT('INV-', DATE_FORMAT(NOW(), '%Y%m%d'), '-', LPAD(v_order_id, 4, '0')),
        v_order_id,
        p_client_id,
        CURDATE(),
        DATE_ADD(CURDATE(), INTERVAL 7 DAY),
        p_final_amount
    );
    
    -- Return order ID
    SELECT v_order_id AS order_id, v_order_number AS order_number;
END//
DELIMITER ;
```

### 4. Tambahkan Fungsi untuk Perhitungan Komisi

```sql
-- Fungsi untuk menghitung komisi freelancer
DELIMITER //
CREATE FUNCTION calculate_freelancer_commission(
    order_id INT,
    commission_rate DECIMAL(5,2)
) RETURNS DECIMAL(15,2)
READS SQL DATA
DETERMINISTIC
BEGIN
    DECLARE total_amount DECIMAL(15,2);
    
    SELECT final_amount INTO total_amount
    FROM orders
    WHERE id = order_id;
    
    RETURN total_amount * (commission_rate / 100);
END//
DELIMITER ;
```

### 5. Optimasi Query dengan Materialized View (jika menggunakan MariaDB 10.6+)

```sql
-- Materialized view untuk laporan bulanan
CREATE TABLE monthly_reports (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    report_month DATE,
    total_orders INT,
    total_revenue DECIMAL(15,2),
    total_clients INT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Procedure untuk update materialized view
DELIMITER //
CREATE PROCEDURE update_monthly_reports()
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO monthly_reports (report_month, total_orders, total_revenue, total_clients)
    SELECT 
        DATE_FORMAT(created_at, '%Y-%m-01') AS report_month,
        COUNT(*) AS total_orders,
        SUM(final_amount) AS total_revenue,
        COUNT(DISTINCT client_id) AS total_clients
    FROM orders
    WHERE created_at >= DATE_FORMAT(NOW(), '%Y-%m-01')
    GROUP BY DATE_FORMAT(created_at, '%Y-%m-01')
    ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE
        total_orders = VALUES(total_orders),
        total_revenue = VALUES(total_revenue),
        total_clients = VALUES(total_clients);
END//
DELIMITER ;
```

## üìä STATISTIK DATABASE

- **Total Tabel:** 17
- **Total Kolom:** 150+
- **Total Relasi:** 20+ foreign key constraints
- **Total Index:** 40+ indexes
- **Total Data Awal:** 100+ records

## üîí REKOMENDASI KEAMANAN

### 1. Tambahkan Enkripsi untuk Data Sensitif

```sql
-- Update tabel users untuk menyimpan encrypted data
ALTER TABLE users 
ADD COLUMN encrypted_phone VARBINARY(255),
ADD COLUMN encrypted_address VARBINARY(255);

-- Update tabel clients untuk enkripsi data sensitif
ALTER TABLE clients 
ADD COLUMN encrypted_phone VARBINARY(255),
ADD COLUMN encrypted_whatsapp VARBINARY(255),
ADD COLUMN encrypted_address VARBINARY(255);
```

### 2. Tambahkan Audit Trail untuk Tabel Kritis

```sql
-- Tabel audit untuk perubahan harga
CREATE TABLE price_audit (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    table_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    record_id INT NOT NULL,
    field_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    old_value DECIMAL(15,2),
    new_value DECIMAL(15,2),
    changed_by INT NOT NULL,
    changed_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    FOREIGN KEY (changed_by) REFERENCES users(id)
);
```

## ‚úÖ STATUS SETELAH IMPLEMENTASI

Setelah menerapkan rekomendasi di atas:
- ‚úÖ Performa query meningkat dengan view dan stored procedure
- ‚úÖ Konsistensi data terjaga dengan trigger
- ‚úÖ Laporan lebih mudah dengan materialized view
- ‚úÖ Perhitungan komisi lebih efisien dengan fungsi
- ‚úÖ Keamanan data sensitif meningkat dengan enkripsi
- ‚úÖ Audit trail lengkap untuk perubahan kritis

## üéØ REKOMENDASI UNTUK PRODUKSI

1. **Implementasi Database Backup Otomatis**
   ```sql
   -- Backup script untuk daily backup
   mysqldump --single-transaction --routines --triggers nrrskfvk_situneo_digital > backup_$(date +%Y%m%d).sql
   ```

2. **Monitoring Query Performance**
   ```sql
   -- Enable slow query log
   SET GLOBAL slow_query_log = 'ON';
   SET GLOBAL long_query_time = 2;
   ```

3. **Implementasi Database Replication**
   - Master-slave replication untuk high availability
   - Read replicas untuk distribusi beban baca

4. **Database Partitioning untuk Tabel Besar**
   ```sql
   -- Partition tabel orders berdasarkan tahun
   ALTER TABLE orders PARTITION BY RANGE (YEAR(created_at)) (
       PARTITION p2024 VALUES LESS THAN (2025),
       PARTITION p2025 VALUES LESS THAN (2026),
       PARTITION pmax VALUES LESS THAN MAXVALUE
   );
   ```

Database ini sudah memiliki struktur yang sangat baik dan siap untuk production. Dengan beberapa optimasi tambahan, performa dan keamanan akan meningkat secara signifikan untuk mendukung pertumbuhan bisnis Situneo Digital.

Apakah Anda ingin saya membantu dengan implementasi rekomendasi ini atau ada aspek tertentu dari database yang ingin kita bahas lebih dalam?

// Get unique categories with count
$categories = [];
foreach($portfolios as $port) {
    $cat = $port['category'];
    if (!isset($categories[$cat])) {
        $categories[$cat] = 0;
    }
    $categories[$cat]++;
}

    <script>
        // Initialize AOS
        AOS.init({
            duration: 1000,
            once: true,
            offset: 100
        });
        
        // Navbar Scroll Effect
        window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
            const navbar = document.querySelector('.navbar-premium');
            const backToTop = document.getElementById('backToTop');
            
            if (window.scrollY > 100) {
                navbar.classList.add('scrolled');
                backToTop.style.display = 'block';
            } else {
                navbar.classList.remove('scrolled');
                backToTop.style.display = 'none';
            }
        });
        
        // Back to Top
        document.getElementById('backToTop').addEventListener('click', function() {
            window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
        });
        
        // Filter Portfolio Function
        function filterPortfolio(category) {
            const items = document.querySelectorAll('.portfolio-item');
            const noResults = document.getElementById('noResults');
            const filterBtns = document.querySelectorAll('.filter-btn');
            let visibleCount = 0;
            
            // Update active button
            filterBtns.forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            
            // Filter items
            items.forEach(item => {
                if (category === 'all' || item.dataset.category === category) {
                    item.style.display = 'block';
                    visibleCount++;
                } else {
                    item.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
            
            // Show/hide no results message
            if (visibleCount === 0) {
                noResults.style.display = 'block';
            } else {
                noResults.style.display = 'none';
            }
            
            // Re-initialize AOS
            AOS.refresh();
        }
        
        // Search Portfolio Function
        function searchPortfolio() {
            const searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput').value.toLowerCase();
            const items = document.querySelectorAll('.portfolio-item');
            const noResults = document.getElementById('noResults');
            let visibleCount = 0;
            
            items.forEach(item => {
                const title = item.dataset.title;
                if (title.includes(searchInput)) {
                    item.style.display = 'block';
                    visibleCount++;
                } else {
                    item.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
            
            // Show/hide no results message
            if (visibleCount === 0) {
                noResults.style.display = 'block';
            } else {
                noResults.style.display = 'none';
            }
        }
        
        // Reset Filter Function
        function resetFilter() {
            document.getElementById('searchInput').value = '';
            const items = document.querySelectorAll('.portfolio-item');
            const noResults = document.getElementById('noResults');
            const filterBtns = document.querySelectorAll('.filter-btn');
            
            // Show all items
            items.forEach(item => {
                item.style.display = 'block';
            });
            
            // Hide no results
            noResults.style.display = 'none';
            
            // Reset active button
            filterBtns.forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
            filterBtns[0].classList.add('active');
        }
        
        // Smooth Scroll
        document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
            anchor.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                const href = this.getAttribute('href');
                if (href !== '#') {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    const target = document.querySelector(href);
                    if (target) {
                        const offset = 100;
                        const targetPosition = target.offsetTop - offset;
                        window.scrollTo({
                            top: targetPosition,
                            behavior: 'smooth'
                        });
                    }
                }
            });
        });
        
        // Network Background Animation
        const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
        const networkBg = document.getElementById('networkBg');
        networkBg.appendChild(canvas);
        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
        
        canvas.width = window.innerWidth;
        canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
        
        const particles = [];
        const particleCount = 80;
        
        class Particle {
            constructor() {
                this.x = Math.random() * canvas.width;
                this.y = Math.random() * canvas.height;
                this.vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;
                this.vy = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;
                this.radius = Math.random() * 2 + 1;
            }
            
            update() {
                this.x += this.vx;
                this.y += this.vy;
                
                if (this.x < 0 || this.x > canvas.width) this.vx *= -1;
                if (this.y < 0 || this.y > canvas.height) this.vy *= -1;
            }
            
            draw() {
                ctx.beginPath();
                ctx.arc(this.x, this.y, this.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
                ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255, 180, 0, 0.5)';
                ctx.fill();
            }
        }
        
        for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
            particles.push(new Particle());
        }
        
        function connectParticles() {
            for (let i = 0; i < particles.length; i++) {
                for (let j = i + 1; j < particles.length; j++) {
                    const dx = particles[i].x - particles[j].x;
                    const dy = particles[i].y - particles[j].y;
                    const distance = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
                    
                    if (distance < 150) {
                        ctx.beginPath();
                        ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(255, 180, 0, ${0.2 * (1 - distance / 150)})`;
                        ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
                        ctx.moveTo(particles[i].x, particles[i].y);
                        ctx.lineTo(particles[j].x, particles[j].y);
                        ctx.stroke();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        function animate() {
            ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
            
            particles.forEach(particle => {
                particle.update();
                particle.draw();
            });
            
            connectParticles();
            requestAnimationFrame(animate);
        }
        
        animate();
        
        window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
            canvas.width = window.innerWidth;
            canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
