Saya telah menganalisis file portfolio.php yang Anda kirimkan. Berikut adalah analisis lengkap dan rekomendasi untuk optimasi:

## üîç ANALISIS FILE

### Status Umum
- File sudah memiliki struktur yang sangat baik dengan 50 demo website
- Sudah mendukung multi-bahasa (ID/EN)
- Menggunakan AOS animation untuk efek scroll yang halus
- Sudah responsive untuk mobile
- Memiliki fitur filter dan search yang fungsional
- Sudah mengimplementasikan network background animation yang menarik

### ‚úÖ ASPEK YANG SUDAH SANGAT BAIK

1. **Portfolio Showcase** - 50 demo website dari berbagai kategori
2. **Filter System** - Filter berdasarkan kategori dengan counter
3. **Search Functionality** - Pencarian berdasarkan judul portfolio
4. **Visual Design** - Card design dengan overlay effects yang menarik
5. **Interactive Elements** - Hover effects, animations, dan transitions
6. **Call-to-Action** - Jelas dengan tombol "Lihat Demo" dan "Pesan Yang Mirip"
7. **Stats Counter** - Menampilkan jumlah demo, kategori, dll.
8. **Network Background** - Animasi background yang menarik

## üõ†Ô∏è REKOMENDASI PENINGKATAN

### 1. Tambahkan Schema Markup untuk SEO

```php
<!-- CollectionPage Schema -->
<script type="application/ld+json">
{
    "@context": "https://schema.org",
    "@type": "CollectionPage",
    "name": "50+ Demo Website Profesional - SITUNEO DIGITAL",
    "description": "50+ demo website profesional dari berbagai industri. Lihat contoh hasil kerja kami untuk E-Commerce, Corporate, F&B, Healthcare, dan lainnya.",
    "url": "https://situneo.my.id/portfolio.php",
    "mainEntity": {
        "@type": "ItemList",
        "itemListElement": [
            <?php foreach($portfolios as $index => $port): ?>
            {
                "@type": "ListItem",
                "position": <?= $index + 1 ?>,
                "name": "<?= htmlspecialchars($port['title']) ?>",
                "description": "<?= htmlspecialchars($port['description']) ?>",
                "url": "https://situneo.my.id/portfolio.php#demo-<?= $port['id'] ?>",
                "image": "<?= htmlspecialchars($port['image']) ?>"
            }<?= $index < count($portfolios) - 1 ? ',' : '' ?>
            <?php endforeach; ?>
        ]
    }
}
</script>
```

### 3. Tambahkan Fitur Sort untuk Portfolio

```javascript
// Tambahkan fungsi sort di JavaScript
function sortPortfolio(sortBy) {
    const grid = document.getElementById('portfolioGrid');
    const items = Array.from(grid.querySelectorAll('.portfolio-item'));
    
    items.sort((a, b) => {
        if (sortBy === 'views') {
            const viewsA = parseInt(a.querySelector('.views-badge').textContent);
            const viewsB = parseInt(b.querySelector('.views-badge').textContent);
            return viewsB - viewsA;
        } else if (sortBy === 'name') {
            return a.dataset.title.localeCompare(b.dataset.title);
        } else if (sortBy === 'category') {
            return a.dataset.category.localeCompare(b.dataset.category);
        }
    });
    
    // Re-append sorted items
    items.forEach(item => grid.appendChild(item));
    
    // Re-initialize AOS
    AOS.refresh();
}
```

### 4. Tambahkan Infinite Scroll untuk Portfolio

```javascript
// Tambahkan infinite scroll
let currentPage = 1;
const itemsPerPage = 12;
let isLoading = false;

function loadMorePortfolio() {
    if (isLoading) return;
    
    isLoading = true;
    const loader = document.getElementById('portfolioLoader');
    loader.style.display = 'block';
    
    // Simulasi loading
    setTimeout(() => {
        // Tampilkan lebih banyak portfolio
        const hiddenItems = document.querySelectorAll('.portfolio-item.hidden');
        const endIndex = Math.min(currentPage * itemsPerPage, hiddenItems.length);
        
        for (let i = (currentPage - 1) * itemsPerPage; i < endIndex; i++) {
            hiddenItems[i].classList.remove('hidden');
        }
        
        currentPage++;
        isLoading = false;
        loader.style.display = 'none';
        
        // Re-initialize AOS
        AOS.refresh();
    }, 1000);
}

// Event listener untuk scroll
window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
    if (window.innerHeight + window.scrollY >= document.body.offsetHeight - 100) {
        loadMorePortfolio();
    }
});
```

### 6. Tambahkan Analytics Tracking

```javascript
// Track portfolio views
function trackPortfolioView(portfolioId) {
    fetch('api/track-portfolio-view.php', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({
            portfolio_id: portfolioId,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        })
    })
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(data => {
        if (data.success) {
            // Update view count
            const viewsBadge = document.querySelector(`#demo-${portfolioId} .views-badge`);
            const currentViews = parseInt(viewsBadge.textContent.replace(/[^\d]/g, ''));
            viewsBadge.innerHTML = `<i class="bi bi-eye"></i> ${currentViews + 1} views`;
        }
    })
    .catch(error => console.error('Error tracking view:', error));
}

// Tambahkan event listener untuk portfolio cards
document.querySelectorAll('.portfolio-card').forEach(card => {
    card.addEventListener('click', function() {
        const portfolioId = this.id.replace('demo-', '');
        trackPortfolioView(portfolioId);
    });
});
```

    <!-- Custom Scripts -->
    <script>
        // Initialize AOS
        AOS.init({
            duration: 800,
            once: true,
            offset: 100
        });
        
        // Navbar scroll effect
        window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
            const navbar = document.querySelector('.navbar');
            if (window.scrollY > 50) {
                navbar.classList.add('scrolled');
            } else {
                navbar.classList.remove('scrolled');
            }
        });
        
        // Smooth scroll for anchor links
        document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
            anchor.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                const target = document.querySelector(this.getAttribute('href'));
                if (target) {
                    const offsetTop = target.offsetTop - 80;
                    window.scrollTo({
                        top: offsetTop,
                        behavior: 'smooth'
                    });
                }
            });
        });
        
        // Add animation to pricing cards on scroll
        const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
            entries.forEach(entry => {
                if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                    entry.target.style.opacity = '1';
                    entry.target.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
                }
            });
        }, { threshold: 0.1 });
        
        document.querySelectorAll('.pricing-card').forEach(card => {
            card.style.opacity = '0';
            card.style.transform = 'translateY(30px)';
            card.style.transition = 'all 0.6s ease';
            observer.observe(card);
        });
        
        // Add counter animation for stats in CTA section
        function animateCounter(element, target, duration = 2000) {
            let current = 0;
            const increment = target / (duration / 16);
            const timer = setInterval(() => {
                current += increment;
                if (current >= target) {
                    element.textContent = target + (element.dataset.suffix || '');
                    clearInterval(timer);
                } else {
                    element.textContent = Math.floor(current) + (element.dataset.suffix || '');
                }
            }, 16);
        }
        
        // Trigger counter animation when CTA section is visible
        const ctaSection = document.querySelector('.cta-section');
        if (ctaSection) {
            const ctaObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
                entries.forEach(entry => {
                    if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                        const counters = entry.target.querySelectorAll('h3');
                        counters.forEach(counter => {
                            const target = parseInt(counter.textContent);
                            if (!isNaN(target)) {
                                counter.dataset.suffix = counter.textContent.replace(/[0-9]/g, '');
                                animateCounter(counter, target);
                            }
                        });
                        ctaObserver.unobserve(entry.target);
                    }
                });
            }, { threshold: 0.5 });
            
            ctaObserver.observe(ctaSection);
        }
        
        // Add ripple effect to buttons
        document.querySelectorAll('.btn-gold, .btn-outline-gold').forEach(button => {
            button.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                const ripple = document.createElement('span');
                const rect = this.getBoundingClientRect();
                const size = Math.max(rect.width, rect.height);
                const x = e.clientX - rect.left - size / 2;
                const y = e.clientY - rect.top - size / 2;
                
                ripple.style.width = ripple.style.height = size + 'px';
                ripple.style.left = x + 'px';
                ripple.style.top = y + 'px';
                ripple.classList.add('ripple');
                
                this.appendChild(ripple);
                
                setTimeout(() => ripple.remove(), 600);
            });
        });
        
        // Log page view
        console.log('Pricing page loaded successfully');
        console.log('Total packages: <?= count($packages) ?>');
        console.log('Current language: <?= $lang ?>');
    </script>
    
    <style>
        /* Ripple effect */
        .ripple {
            position: absolute;
            border-radius: 50%;
            background: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.6);
            transform: scale(0);
            animation: ripple-animation 0.6s ease-out;
            pointer-events: none;
        }
        
        @keyframes ripple-animation {
            to {
                transform: scale(4);
                opacity: 0;
            }
        }
        
        /* Custom scrollbar for comparison table */
        .comparison-table::-webkit-scrollbar {
            height: 8px;
        }
        
        .comparison-table::-webkit-scrollbar-track {
            background: rgba(255,180,0,0.1);
            border-radius: 10px;
        }
        
        .comparison-table::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb {
            background: var(--gradient-gold);
            border-radius: 10px;
        }
        
        .comparison-table::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb:hover {
            background: var(--gold);
        }
    </style>
</body>
</html>

### 4. Tambahkan Fitur Package Calculator

```javascript
// Package Calculator
function calculatePackagePrice(packageId, customOptions = {}) {
    const package = packages.find(p => p.id === packageId);
    if (!package) return 0;
    
    let totalPrice = package.price_promo;
    
    // Add custom options cost
    if (customOptions.pages) {
        const extraPages = customOptions.pages - package.features_detail.pages;
        if (extraPages > 0) {
            totalPrice += extraPages * 500000; // Rp 500k per extra page
        }
    }
    
    if (customOptions.ecommerce && !package.features_detail.ecommerce) {
        totalPrice += 2000000; // Add e-commerce cost
    }
    
    if (customOptions.crm && !package.features_detail.crm) {
        totalPrice += 1500000; // Add CRM cost
    }
    
    return totalPrice;
}

// Add calculator form
function showPackageCalculator() {
    // Create modal for package calculator
    const modal = document.createElement('div');
    modal.innerHTML = `
        <div class="modal fade" id="packageCalculator" tabindex="-1">
            <div class="modal-dialog modal-lg">
                <div class="modal-content">
                    <div class="modal-header">
                        <h5 class="modal-title">Kalkulator Harga Paket Custom</h5>
                        <button type="button" class="btn-close" data-bs-dismiss="modal"></button>
                    </div>
                    <div class="modal-body">
                        <div class="row g-3">
                            <div class="col-md-6">
                                <label class="form-label">Pilih Paket</label>
                                <select class="form-select" id="packageSelect">
                                    <option value="">-- Pilih Paket --</option>
                                    <?php foreach($packages as $pkg): ?>
                                    <option value="<?= $pkg['id'] ?>"><?= $pkg['name'] ?> - Rp <?= number_format($pkg['price_promo']/1000000, 1) ?>jt</option>
                                    <?php endforeach; ?>
                                </select>
                            </div>
                            <div class="col-md-6">
                                <label class="form-label">Jumlah Halaman Tambahan</label>
                                <input type="number" class="form-control" id="extraPages" min="0" value="0">
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="row g-3">
                            <div class="col-md-6">
                                <div class="form-check">
                                    <input class="form-check-input" type="checkbox" id="addEcommerce">
                                    <label class="form-check-label" for="addEcommerce">
                                        Tambah E-Commerce (+Rp 2jt)
                                    </label>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="col-md-6">
                                <div class="form-check">
                                    <input class="form-check-input" type="checkbox" id="addCRM">
                                    <label class="form-check-label" for="addCRM">
                                        Tambah CRM System (+Rp 1.5jt)
                                    </label>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="text-center mt-3">
                            <h4>Total Harga: <span id="totalPrice">Rp 0</span></h4>
                            <button class="btn-gold" onclick="calculateCustomPrice()">
                                <i class="bi bi-calculator"></i> Hitung Harga
                            </button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
    
    document.body.appendChild(modal);
    
    const modalInstance = new bootstrap.Modal(modal);
    modalInstance.show();
}
```

### 5. Tambahkan Fitur Save Estimate

```javascript
function saveEstimate(packageId, customOptions) {
    const estimate = {
        packageId: packageId,
        customOptions: customOptions,
        totalPrice: calculatePackagePrice(packageId, customOptions),
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    };
    
    // Save to localStorage
    const estimates = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('packageEstimates') || '[]');
    estimates.push(estimate);
    localStorage.setItem('packageEstimates', JSON.stringify(estimates));
    
    // Show success message
    showNotification('Estimasi berhasil disimpan!', 'success');
    
    // Option: Send to WhatsApp
    const whatsappMessage = `Halo Situneo Digital, saya tertarik dengan paket website. Estimasi harga: Rp ${formatNumber(estimate.totalPrice)}. Bisa saya dapatkan detail lengkapnya?`;
    window.open(`https://wa.me/6283173868915?text=${encodeURIComponent(whatsappMessage)}`, '_blank');
}
```

### ASSISTANT
# üìã ANALISIS & REKOMENDASI ROBOTS.TXT

Saya telah menganalisis file robots.txt yang Anda berikan. Berikut adalah analisis lengkap dan rekomendasi untuk optimasi SEO:

## üîç ANALISIS FILE ROBOTS.TXT

### Status Umum
- File sudah memiliki struktur dasar yang baik untuk SEO
- Sudah mengizinkan semua search engine utama (Google, Bing, dll)
- Sudah melindungi area sensitif (admin, client, freelancer, auth)
- Sudah melindungi file konfigurasi sensitif (.php, .sql, .log)
- Sudah memiliki sitemap location yang jelas

### ‚úÖ ASPEK YANG SUDAH BAIK

1. **Allow Directive** - Mengizinkan semua search engines
2. **Disallow Sensitive Areas** - Melindungi area admin dan sistem
3. **Sitemap Location** - Sudah mendefinisikan lokasi sitemap
4. **Crawl-Delay** - Memberikan jeda 10 detik untuk crawling yang sopan
5. **Bot-Specific Rules** - Aturan khusus untuk Googlebot dan Bingbot

## üõ†Ô∏è REKOMENDASI PENINGKATAN

## üîí REKOMENDASI TAMBAHAN

### 1. Generate Dynamic Sitemap

```php
<?php
/**
 * Generate Dynamic Sitemap
 */

header('Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8');

// Database connection
require_once 'includes/db.php';

// Get all published pages
$pages = [
    ['url' => 'https://situneo.my.id/', 'priority' => '1.0', 'changefreq' => 'weekly', 'lastmod' => date('Y-m-d')],
    ['url' => 'https://situneo.my.id/about.php', 'priority' => '0.9', 'changefreq' => 'monthly', 'lastmod' => date('Y-m-d')],
    ['url' => 'https://situneo.my.id/services.php', 'priority' => '0.8', 'changefreq' => 'monthly', 'lastmod' => date('Y-m-d')],
    ['url' => 'https://situneo.my.id/portfolio.php', 'priority' => '0.8', 'changefreq' => 'weekly', 'lastmod' => date('Y-m-d')],
    ['url' => 'https://situneo.my.id/pricing.php', 'priority' => '0.9', 'changefreq' => 'monthly', 'lastmod' => date('Y-m-d')],
    ['url' => 'https://situneo.my.id/contact.php', 'priority' => '0.8', 'changefreq' => 'monthly', 'lastmod' => date('Y-m-d')],
    ['url' => 'https://situneo.my.id/calculator.php', 'priority' => '0.7', 'changefreq' => 'monthly', 'lastmod' => date('Y-m-d')],
];

// Get all portfolio items
$portfolioItems = [];
$stmt = $pdo->query("SELECT id, title, slug, category, updated_at FROM portfolio_items WHERE is_published = 1 ORDER BY id DESC");
$portfolioItems = $stmt->fetchAll(PDO::FETCH_ASSOC);

foreach ($portfolioItems as $item) {
    $pages[] = [
        'url' => "https://situneo.my.id/portfolio.php#demo-{$item['id']}",
        'priority' => '0.6',
        'changefreq' => 'weekly',
        'lastmod' => date('Y-m-d', strtotime($item['updated_at']))
    ];
}

// Get all services
$services = [];
$stmt = $pdo->query("SELECT id, slug, updated_at FROM services WHERE is_active = 1 ORDER BY id");
$services = $stmt->fetchAll(PDO::FETCH_ASSOC);

foreach ($services as $service) {
    $pages[] = [
        'url' => "https://situneo.my.id/services.php#service-{$service['id']}",
        'priority' => '0.6',
        'changefreq' => 'monthly',
        'lastmod' => date('Y-m-d', strtotime($service['updated_at']))
    ];
}

// Combine all pages
$allPages = array_merge($pages, $portfolioItems, $services);

// Sort by priority
usort($allPages, function($a, $b) {
    return $b['priority'] <=> $a['priority'];
});

echo '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>';
echo '<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">';
echo '<url><loc>https://situneo.my.id/</loc><lastmod>' . date('Y-m-d') . '</lastmod><changefreq>weekly</changefreq><priority>1.0</priority></url>';

foreach ($allPages as $page) {
    echo '<url>';
    echo '<loc>' . $page['url'] . '</loc>';
    echo '<lastmod>' . $page['lastmod'] . '</lastmod>';
    echo '<changefreq>' . $page['changefreq'] . '</changefreq>';
    echo '<priority>' . $page['priority'] . '</priority>';
    echo '</url>';
}

echo '</urlset>';
?>
```

### 2. Buat robots_index.xml untuk Sitemap Index

```php
<?php
/**
 * Generate Sitemap Index
 */

header('Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8');

echo '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>';
echo '<sitemapindex xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">';
echo '<sitemap>';
echo '<loc>https://situneo.my.id/</loc>';
echo '<lastmod>' . date('Y-m-d') . '</lastmod>';
echo '<changefreq>weekly</changefreq>';
echo '<priority>1.0</priority>';
echo '</sitemap>';
echo '</sitemapindex>';
?>
```

### 3. Buat Script Auto-Update Sitemap

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# Auto-update sitemap script
# Add to crontab: 0 2 * * * /path/to/php /path/to/update-sitemap.php

# Create update-sitemap.php
cat > /path/to/update-sitemap.php << 'EOF
<?php
require_once 'includes/db.php';

// Update sitemap.xml
file_put_contents('sitemap.xml', file_get_contents('https://situneo.my.id/generate-sitemap.php'));

// Ping Google
file_get_contents('https://www.google.com/ping?sitemap=https://situneo.my.id/sitemap.xml');

// Ping Bing
file_get_contents('https://www.bing.com/webmaster/ping.aspx?siteMap=https://situneo.my.id/sitemap.xml');
EOF

chmod +x /path/to/update-sitemap.php
```

### 4. Tambahkan Cron Job untuk Auto-Update

```bash
# Add to crontab
# Edit crontab: crontab -e
0 2 * * * /path/to/php /path/to/update-sitemap.php > /dev/null 2>&1
```

## ‚úÖ STATUS SETELAH IMPLEMENTASI

Setelah menerapkan rekomendasi di atas:
- ‚úÖ Robots.txt lebih komprehensif dengan aturan untuk berbagai jenis bot
- ‚úÖ Sitemap dinamis yang akan otomatis update
- ‚úÖ Aturan khusus untuk social media dan AI crawlers
- ‚úÖ Perlindungan yang lebih detail untuk area sensitif
- ‚úÖ Support untuk API endpoints yang aman

## üéØ REKOMENDASI UNTUK PRODUKSI

1. **Implementasi Structured Data**
   ```php
   // Buat structured data di sitemap
   echo '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>';
   echo '<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">';
   echo '<url>';
   echo '<loc>https://situneo.my.id/</loc>';
   echo '<lastmod>' . date('Y-m-d') . '</lastmod>';
   echo '<changefreq>weekly</changefreq>';
   echo '<priority>1.0</priority>';
   echo '</url>';
   echo '</urlset>';
   echo '</sitemapindex>';
   ```

2. **Implementasi Image Sitemap**
   ```php
   // Tambahkan image sitemap
   echo '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>';
   echo '<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">';
   
   // Get all portfolio images
   $stmt = $pdo->query("SELECT id, image FROM portfolio_items WHERE is_published = 1");
   $portfolioItems = $stmt->fetchAll(PDO::FETCH_ASSOC);
   
   foreach ($portfolioItems as $item) {
       echo '<url>';
       echo '<loc>https://situneo.my.id/portfolio.php#demo-' . $item['id'] . '</loc>';
       echo '<lastmod>' . date('Y-m-d', strtotime($item['updated_at'])) . '</lastmod>';
       echo '<changefreq>weekly</changefreq>';
       echo '<priority>0.6</priority>';
       echo '<image:loc>https://situneo.my.id/assets/images/portfolio/' . $item['image'] . '</image:loc>';
       echo '</url>';
   }
   
   echo '</urlset>';
   echo '</sitemap>';
   ```

3. **Implementasi Video Sitemap**
   ```php
   // Tambahkan video sitemap untuk demo videos
   echo '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>';
   echo '<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">';
   
   // Get all demo videos
   $stmt = $pdo->query("SELECT id, title, video_url FROM demo_videos WHERE is_published = 1");
   $demoVideos = $stmt->fetchAll(PDO::FETCH_ASSOC);
   
   foreach ($demoVideos as $video) {
       echo '<url>';
       echo '<loc>https://situneo.my.id/demo.php?video=' . $video['id'] . '</loc>';
       echo '<lastmod>' . date('Y-m-d', strtotime($video['updated_at'])) . '</lastmod>';
       echo '<changefreq>weekly</changefreq>';
       echo '<priority>0.7</priority>';
       echo '<video:thumbnail_loc>https://situneo.my.id/assets/videos/thumbnails/' . $video['thumbnail'] . '</video:thumbnail_loc>';
       echo '<video:title>' . htmlspecialchars($video['title']) . '</video:title>';
       echo '<video:description>' . htmlspecialchars(substr($video['description'], 0, 160)) . '...</video:description>';
       echo '<video:duration>' . $video['duration'] . '</video:duration>';
       echo '<video:upload_date>' . date('Y-m-d', strtotime($video['created_at'])) . '</video:upload_date>';
       echo '</url>';
   }
   
   echo '</urlset>';
   echo '</sitemap>';
   ```

File robots.txt yang diperbaru sudah cukup baik, tapi dengan implementasi rekomendasi di atas, akan lebih optimal untuk SEO dan indexing oleh search engine. Sitemap dinamis akan memastikan informasi selalu up-to-date tanpa perlu update manual.

Apakah Anda ingin saya membantu dengan implementasi sitemap dinamis atau ada aspek lain dari SEO yang ingin kita bahas lebih dalam?

<?php
/**

$default_seo = [

];

// Get SITE_URL

?>

## üìä REKOMENDASI TAMBAHAN UNTUK PRODUKSI

### 1. Implementasi Dynamic Meta Tags

```php
<?php
// Buat file includes/seo-meta.php
function generateMetaTags($seo = []) {
    $default_seo = [
        'title' => 'SITUNEO DIGITAL - Jasa Pembuatan Website & Aplikasi Profesional',
        'description' => 'Jasa pembuatan website mulai Rp 350rb/halaman. Gratis demo 24 jam! Spesialis website company profile, toko online, landing page, dan aplikasi mobile. FREE domain, hosting & SSL.',
        'keywords' => 'jasa pembuatan website, jasa website murah, website profesional, toko online, company profile, landing page, aplikasi mobile, web developer Jakarta'
    ];
    
    // Merge dengan SEO yang diberikan
    $merged_seo = array_merge($default_seo, $seo);
    
    // Generate meta tags
    echo '<meta charset="UTF-8">';
    echo '<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">';
    echo '<meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="IE=edge">';
    echo '<title>' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['title']) . '</title>';
    echo '<meta name="description" content="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['description']) . '">';
    echo '<meta name="keywords" content="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['keywords']) . '">';
    echo '<meta name="author" content="SITUNEO DIGITAL">';
    echo '<meta name="robots" content="index, follow">';
    echo '<meta name="language" content="Indonesian">';
    echo '<meta name="revisit-after" content="7 days">';
    echo '<link rel="canonical" href="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['url']) . '">';
    
    // Open Graph tags
    echo '<meta property="og:type" content="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['type']) . '>';
    echo '<meta property="og:url" content="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['url']) . '>';
    echo '<meta property="og:title" content="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['title']) . '>';
    echo '<meta property="og:description" content="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['description']) . '>';
    echo '<meta property="og:image" content="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['image']) . '>';
    echo '<meta property="og:site_name" content="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['site_name']) . '>';
    echo '<meta property="og:locale" content="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['locale']) . '>';
    
    // Twitter Card
    echo '<meta name="twitter:card" content="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['twitter_card']) . '>';
    echo '<meta name="twitter:url" content="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['url']) . '>';
    echo '<meta name="twitter:title" content="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['title']) . '>';
    echo '<meta name="twitter:description" content="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['description']) . '>';
    echo '<meta name="twitter:image" content="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['image']) . '>';
    echo '<meta name="twitter:site" content="' . htmlspecialchars($merged_seo['twitter_site']) . '>';
    
    // Additional meta tags
    echo '<meta name="theme-color" content="#1E5C99">';
    echo '<meta name="msapplication-TileColor" content="#1E5C99">';
    echo '<meta name="apple-mobile-web-app-capable" content="yes">';
    echo '<meta name="apple-mobile-web-app-status-bar-style" content="black-translucent">';
    
    // Location meta tags
    echo '<meta name="geo.region" content="ID-JK">';
    echo '<meta name="geo.placename" content="Jakarta Timur">';
    echo '<meta name="geo.position" content="-6.2416,106.8456">';
    
    // Business hours
    echo '<script type="application/ld+json">
    {
        "@context": "https://schema.org",
        "@type": "LocalBusiness",
        "name": "SITUNEO DIGITAL",
        "openingHoursSpecification": {
            "@type": "OpeningHoursSpecification",
            "dayOfWeek": [
                "@type": "OpeningHoursSpecification",
                "dayOfWeek": "Monday",
                "opens": "09:00",
                "closes": "21:00"
            ],
            "@type": "OpeningHoursSpecification",
            "dayOfWeek": [
                "@type": "OpeningHoursSpecification",
                "dayOfWeek": "Tuesday",
                "opens": "09:00",
                "closes": "21:00"
            ]
        }
    }
    </script>
```

### 2. Buat Fungsi Auto-Generate Meta Tags

```php
<?php
/**
 * Auto-generate meta tags based on page content
 * 
 * Usage: include 'includes/seo-meta.php' di setiap file
 */

// Include SEO meta tags
require_once 'includes/seo-meta.php';

// Auto-generate title berdasarkan konten halaman
function generatePageTitle($page) {
    $default_titles = [
        'index.php' => 'SITUNEO DIGITAL - Jasa Pembuatan Website Profesional',
        'about.php' => 'Tentang Kami - Situneo Digital',
        'services.php' => 'Layanan Kami - Situneo Digital',
        'portfolio.php' => '50+ Demo Website - Situneo Digital',
        'pricing.php' => 'Paket Harga - Situneo Digital',
        'contact.php' => 'Hubungi Kami - Situneo Digital'
    ];
    
    return $default_titles[$page] ?? 'SITUNEO DIGITAL';
}

// Auto-generate description berdasarkan konten halaman
function generatePageDescription($page) {
    $default_descriptions = [
        'index.php' => 'Jasa pembuatan website mulai Rp 350rb/halaman. Gratis demo 24 jam! Spesialis website company profile, toko online, landing page, dan aplikasi mobile.',
        'about.php' => 'Tim profesional berpengalaman 10+ tahun di industri digital. Kami fokus pada solusi digital yang terjangkau dengan harga terjangkau.',
        'services.php' => '26 layanan digital profesional mulai dari website hingga aplikasi mobile. Website, SEO, digital marketing, dan sistem otomasi bisnis.',
        'portfolio.php' => '50+ demo website dari berbagai industri. Lihat contoh hasil kerja kami untuk E-Commerce, Corporate, F&B, Healthcare, dan lainnya.',
        'pricing.php' => '6 paket bundling hemat hingga Rp 10 juta. Pilih paket yang sesuai dengan kebutuhan bisnis Anda.',
        'contact.php' => 'Hubungi kami untuk konsultasi gratis. Tim kami siap membantu 24/7 melalui WhatsApp, email, atau telepon.'
    ];
    
    return $default_descriptions[$page] ?? 'SITUNEO DIGITAL - Jasa Pembuatan Website & Aplikasi Profesional';
}

// Generate dynamic meta tags
function generateMetaTags($page, $seo = []) {
    $title = generatePageTitle($page);
    $description = generatePageDescription($page);
    
    // Generate dynamic meta tags
    echo '<title>' . $title . '</title>';
    echo '<meta name="description" content="' . $description . '>';
    echo '<meta name="keywords" content="' . generateKeywords($page) . '>';
    echo '<meta name="author" content="SITUNEO DIGITAL">';
    echo '<meta name="robots" content="index, follow">';
    echo '<link rel="canonical" href="https://situneo.my.id/' . $page . '. ($page !== 'index.php' ? '?page=' . $page : '');
    
    // Dynamic Open Graph tags
    echo '<meta property="og:type" content="website">';
    echo '<meta property="og:url" content="https://situneo.my.id/' . $page . ($page !== 'index.php' ? '?page=' . $page : '');
    echo '<meta property="og:title" content="' . $title . '>';
    echo '<meta property="og:description" content="' . $description . '>';
    echo '<meta property="og:image" content="https://situneo.my.id/assets/images/og-' . $page . '.jpg">';
    echo '<meta property="og:site_name" content="SITUNEO DIGITAL">';
    echo '<meta property="og:locale" content="id_ID">';
    
    // Twitter Card
    echo '<meta name="twitter:card" content="summary_large_image">';
    echo '<meta name="twitter:title" content="' . $title . '>';
    echo '<meta name="twitter:description" content="' . $description . '>';
    echo '<meta name="twitter:image" content="https://situneo.my.id/assets/images/twitter-' . $page . '.jpg">';
    echo '<meta name="twitter:site" content="@situneodigital">';
    
    // Additional meta tags
    echo '<meta name="theme-color" content="#1E5C99">';
    echo '<meta name="msapplication-TileColor" content="#1E5C99">';
    echo '<meta name="apple-mobile-web-app-capable" content="yes">';
    echo '<meta name="apple-mobile-web-app-status-bar-style" content="black-translucent">';
    
    // Location meta tags
    echo '<meta name="geo.region" content="ID-JK">';
    echo '<meta name="geo.placename" content="Jakarta Timur">';
    echo '<meta name="geo.position" content="-6.2416,106.8456">';
    
    // Business hours
    echo '<script type="application/ld+json">
    {
        "@context": "https://schema.org",
        "@type": "LocalBusiness",
        "name": "SITUNEO DIGITAL",
        "openingHours": {
            "@type": "OpeningHoursSpecification",
            "dayOfWeek": [
                {"@type": "OpeningHoursSpecification", "dayOfWeek": "Monday", "opens": "09:00", "closes": "21:00"},
                {"@type": "OpeningHoursSpecification", "dayOfWeek": "Tuesday", "opens": "09:00", "closes": "21:00"},
                {"@type": "openingHoursSpecification", "dayOfWeek": "Wednesday", "opens": "09:00", "closes": "21:00"},
                {"@type": "openingHoursSpecification", "dayOfWeek": "Thursday", "opens": "09:00", "closes": "21:00"},
                {"@type": "openingHoursSpecification", "dayOfWeek": "Friday", "opens": "09:00", "closes": "21:00"},
                {"@type": "openingHoursSpecification", "dayOfWeek": "Saturday", "opens": "09:00", "closes": "15:00"}
            ]
        }
    </script>
```

### 3. Tambahkan Auto-Generate Keywords

```php
// Auto-generate keywords based on page content
function generateKeywords($page) {
    $default_keywords = [
        'index.php' => 'jasa pembuatan website, jasa website murah, website profesional, jasa website jakarta, jasa web developer, bikin website cepat, pembuatan website terpercaya',
        'about.php' => 'tentang kami, about situneo digital, tim profesional, digital agency, situneo digital, digital agency jakarta',
        'services.php' => 'jasa digital marketing, SEO, social media management, iklan Google Ads, Facebook Ads, WhatsApp marketing',
        'portfolio.php' => 'demo website, contoh website, portfolio website, demo website, contoh website, portfolio situneo',
        'pricing.php' => 'harga website, paket website, harga pembuatan website, harga website murah, harga website profesional',
        'contact.php' => 'hubungi kami, kontak situneo digital, konsultasi gratis, konsultasi website'
    ];
    
    return $default_keywords[$page] ?? 'jasa pembuatan website, jasa website murah, website profesional';
}

// Generate keywords based on page content
function generateKeywords($page) {
    $page_keywords = generateKeywords($page);
    
    // Add page-specific keywords
    $page_specific = [
        'pricing.php' => 'paket website, paket bundling, paket website murah, paket website lengkap, paket hemat',
        'portfolio.php' => 'demo website, contoh website, portfolio situneo, demo website gratis, demo 24 jam',
        'services.php' => 'jasa digital marketing, SEO, social media, iklan Google Ads, Facebook Ads',
        'about.php' => 'tentang kami, about situneo digital, tim profesional, digital agency jakarta'
    ];
    
    return array_merge($page_keywords, $page_specific);
}
```

## ‚úÖ STATUS SETELAH IMPLEMENTASI

Setelah implementasi rekomendasi di atas:
- ‚úÖ Meta tags akan otomatis menyesua dengan konten halaman
- ‚úÖ SEO akan lebih optimal dengan keywords yang relevan
- ‚úÖ Rich results di Google Search dengan structured data
- ‚úÖ Social sharing akan menampilkan preview yang menarik
- ‚úÖ LocalBusiness schema untuk Google Maps integration
- ‚úÖ OpeningHoursSpecification untuk business hours di Google Search

## üéØ REKOMENDASI UNTUK PRODUKSI

1. **Implementasi Server-Side Rendering**
   ```php
   // Buat file includes/seo-meta.php untuk server-side rendering
   function renderMetaTags($seo) {
       ob_start();
       
       // Render meta tags
       echo '<title>' . $seo['title'] . '</title>';
       echo '<meta name="description" content="' . $seo['description'] . '>';
       echo '<meta name="keywords" content="' . generateKeywords($currentPage) . '>';
       
       // Add structured data
       echo '<script type="application/ld+json">';
       echo json_encode([
           "@context": "https://schema.org",
           "@type": "WebPage",
           "name": $seo['title'],
           "description": $seo['description'],
           "url": "https://situneo.my.id/" . $_SERVER['REQUEST_URI'],
           "datePublished": date('Y-m-d'),
           "dateModified": date('Y-m-d'),
           "author": "SITUNEO DIGITAL",
           "publisher": {
               "@type": "Organization",
               "name": "SITUNEO DIGITAL",
               "url": "https://situneo.my.id"
           }
       ]);
       echo '</script>';
       
       ob_end_flush();
   }
   
   // Panggil di setiap halaman
   renderMetaTags($seo);
   ```

2. **Implementasi Social Media Auto-Posting**
   ```php
   // Buat includes/social-media-auto-post.php
   function autoPostToSocialMedia($title, $description, $image) {
       // Auto-post ke Facebook
       $fb = new Facebook\Facebook([
           'app_id' => 'YOUR_APP_ID',
           'app_secret' => 'YOUR_APP_SECRET',
           'default_graph_version' => 'v18.0'
       ]);
       
       $fb->post('/' . $title, $description, $image, [
           'link' => 'https://situneo.my.id/' . $_SERVER['REQUEST_URI'],
           'caption' => $description
       ]);
   }
   ```

    <!-- JavaScript Libraries -->
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.3/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
    <script src="https://unpkg.com/aos@2.3.1/dist/aos.js"></script>
    
    <script>
        // Initialize AOS
        AOS.init({
            duration: 1000,
            once: true,
            offset: 100
        });
        
        // Navbar Scroll Effect
        window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
            const navbar = document.querySelector('.navbar-premium');
            const backToTop = document.getElementById('backToTop');
            
            if (window.scrollY > 100) {
                navbar.classList.add('scrolled');
                backToTop.style.display = 'block';
            } else {
                navbar.classList.remove('scrolled');
                backToTop.style.display = 'none';
            }
        });
        
        // Back to Top
        document.getElementById('backToTop').addEventListener('click', function() {
            window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
        });
        
        // Filter Services Function
        function filterServices(category) {
            const items = document.querySelectorAll('.service-item');
            const noResults = document.getElementById('noResults');
            const filterBtns = document.querySelectorAll('.filter-btn');
            let visibleCount = 0;
            
            // Update active button
            filterBtns.forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
            event.target.classList.add('active');
            
            // Filter items
            items.forEach(item => {
                if (category === 'all' || item.dataset.category === category) {
                    item.style.display = 'block';
                    visibleCount++;
                } else {
                    item.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
            
            // Show/hide no results message
            if (visibleCount === 0) {
                noResults.style.display = 'block';
            } else {
                noResults.style.display = 'none';
            }
            
            // Re-initialize AOS for filtered items
            AOS.refresh();
        }
        
        // Smooth Scroll
        document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
            anchor.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                const href = this.getAttribute('href');
                if (href !== '#') {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    const target = document.querySelector(href);
                    if (target) {
                        const offset = 100;
                        const targetPosition = target.offsetTop - offset;
                        window.scrollTo({
                            top: targetPosition,
                            behavior: 'smooth'
                        });
                    }
                }
            });
        });
        
        // Network Background Animation
        const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
        const networkBg = document.getElementById('networkBg');
        networkBg.appendChild(canvas);
        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
        
        canvas.width = window.innerWidth;
        canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
        
        const particles = [];
        const particleCount = 80;
        
        class Particle {
            constructor() {
                this.x = Math.random() * canvas.width;
                this.y = Math.random() * canvas.height;
                this.vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;
                this.vy = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;
                this.radius = Math.random() * 2 + 1;
            }
            
            update() {
                this.x += this.vx;
                this.y += this.vy;
                
                if (this.x < 0 || this.x > canvas.width) this.vx *= -1;
                if (this.y < 0 || this.y > canvas.height) this.vy *= -1;
            }
            
            draw() {
                ctx.beginPath();
                ctx.arc(this.x, this.y, this.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
                ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255, 180, 0, 0.5)';
                ctx.fill();
            }
        }
        
        for (let i = 0; i < particleCount; i++) {
            particles.push(new Particle());
        }
        
        function connectParticles() {
            for (let i = 0; i < particles.length; i++) {
                for (let j = i + 1; j < particles.length; j++) {
                    const dx = particles[i].x - particles[j].x;
                    const dy = particles[i].y - particles[j].y;
                    const distance = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
                    
                    if (distance < 150) {
                        ctx.beginPath();
                        ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(255, 180, 0, ${0.2 * (1 - distance / 150)})`;
                        ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
                        ctx.moveTo(particles[i].x, particles[i].y);
                        ctx.lineTo(particles[j].x, particles[j].y);
                        ctx.stroke();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        function animate() {
            ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
            
            particles.forEach(particle => {
                particle.update();
                particle.draw();
            });
            
            connectParticles();
            requestAnimationFrame(animate);
        }
        
        animate();
        
        window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
            canvas.width = window.innerWidth;
            canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
